nainaṃ devā āpuḥ pitaro nota martyāḥ । tasmai te kāma nāma it kṛṇomi ।। nāgniḥ sūryo nota candramāḥ । ।।
nāhorātrāṇi vihitāni yanti । ।। na gandharvāpsaraso na sarpāḥ । tasmai te kāma nama it kṛṇomi ।।
yāvad āpaḥ siṣyadur yāvad agniḥ । tasmai te kāma nama it kṛṇomi ।। yāvatīr āśā abhicakṣaṇā divaḥ । tasmai te kāma nama it kṛṇomi ।।
yāvatīr vaghā vṛkṣasarpyaḥ । tasmai te kāma nama it kṛṇomi ।। yābhiḥ satyaṃ bhavati yad vṛṇīte । -anyatra pāpīr apa veśayā dhiyaḥ ।।
jātāyāḥ pativedanau । aliṃśa uta vatsapaḥ ।। kokaṃ malimrucaṃ palījakam । muṣkayor apa hanmasi ।।
ūrū māva sṛpo antarā । bajaṃ durṇāmacātanam ।। -ubhau saṃvṛtam icchataḥ । sunāmā straiṇam icchatām ।।
stambajā uta taṇḍikaḥ । muṣkayor apa hanmasi ।। kravyādam uta reriham । bajaḥ piṅgo anīnaśat ।।
yaś ca dipsati jāgratīm । parikrāmam anīnaśat ।। bhrātā bhūtvā piteva ca । klībarūpaṃ tirīṭinam ।।
mṛtavatsām imāṃ striyam । -asyāḥ kamalam añjivam ।। kakubhāḥ saramāḥ sumāḥ । viṣūcīnān vi nāśaya ।।
kṛttīr dūrśāni bibhrati । tān ito nāśayāmasi ।। puraḥ pārṣṇī puro mukham । kumbhamuṣkā ayāśavaḥ ।
pratībodhena nāśaya ।। ātapantam amuṃ divaḥ । makakān nāśayāmasi ।। snuṣeva śvaśurād adhi ।
hṛdaye adhi ni vidhyatām ।। aṃśa ādhāya bibhrati । indra rakṣāṃsi nāśaya ।। haste śṛṅgāṇi bibhrataḥ ।
tān ito nāśayāmasi ।। straiṇāḥ santu paṇḍagāḥ । apatiḥ svapatīṃ striyam ।। jambhayantaṃ marīmṛśam ।
tuṇḍenam uta śāluḍam । sthālīṃ gaur iva syandanā ।। jātaṃ vā mārayāti te । kṛṇotu hṛdayāvidham ।।
sūtikā anuśerate । abhraṃ vāta ivājatu ।। yad dhitaṃ māva pādi tat । bheṣajau nīvibhāryau ।।
rakṣasām asi cātanam । viṣūcīnān vi nāśaya ।। chāyakād uta nagnakāt । pari pātu kimīdinaḥ ।।
pañcapādād anaṅguleḥ । pari pāhi varīvṛtāt ।। garbhān khādanti keśavāḥ । muṣkayor apa hanmasi ।।
pumāṃsaṃ mā striyaṃ kran । bādhasvetaḥ kimīdinaḥ ।। ād rodam agham āvayam । -apriye prati muñca tat ।।
durgandhīṃl lohitāsyān । viṣvañco yantu nirhatāḥ ।। anuvāka ।। ucchiṣṭe loka āhitaḥ ।
viśvam antaḥ samāhitam ।। viśvaṃ bhūtaṃ samāhitam । candramā vāta āhitaḥ ।। mṛtyur vājaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।
vraś ca draś cāpi śrīr mayi ।। brahma viśvasṛjo daśa । ucchiṣṭe devatā hitā ।। udgīthaḥ prastutaṃ sthitam ।
sāmno meḍiś ca tan mayi ।। mahānāmnīr mahāvratam । antar garbha iva mātari ।। agniṣṭomas tadadhvaraḥ ।
jīvabarhir madintamaḥ ।। kāmapraś chandasā saha । ucchiṣṭe adhi samāhitāḥ ।। vaṣaṭkāro vrataṃ tapaḥ ।
-ucchiṣṭe adhi samāhitāḥ ।। sadyaḥkrīḥ prakrīr ukthyaḥ । yajñasyāṇūni vidyayā ।। ṣaḍrātraś cobhayaḥ saha ।
ye yajñā amṛte hitāḥ ।। viśvajic cābhijic ca yaḥ । dvādaśāho api tan mayi ।। svadhorjāmṛtaṃ sahaḥ ।
kāmāḥ kāmena tṛpyantu ।। -ucchiṣṭe adhi śritā divaḥ । ahorātre ca tan mayi ।। ye ca yajñā guhā hitāḥ ।
-ucchiṣṭo janituḥ pitā ।। asoḥ pautraḥ pitāmahaḥ । vṛṣā bhūmyām atighnyaḥ ।। śramo dharmaś ca karma ca ।
vīryaṃ lakṣmīr balaṃ bale ।। kṣatraṃ rāṣṭraṃ ṣaḍ urvyaḥ । iḍā praiṣā grahā haviḥ ।। caturmāsyāni nividaḥ ।
paśubandhās tad iṣṭayaḥ ।। -ārtava ṛtubhiḥ saha । stanayitnuḥ śrutir mahī ।। oṣadhayo vīrudhas tṛṇā ।
ucchiṣṭe saṃśritā śritā ।। samāptir maha edhatuḥ । āhitā nihitā hitā ।। yac ca paśyati cakṣuṣā ।
divi devā diviśritaḥ ।। akṣitiś ca kṣitiś ca yā । ।। gandharvāpasaraś ca ye ।
।। purāṇaṃ yajuṣā saha । ।। sarpapuṇyajanāś ca ye ।
।। -abhīmodamudaś ca ye । divi devā diviśritaḥ ।। saṃkalpasya gṛhād adhi ।
ka u jyeṣṭhavaro abhavat ।। -antar mahaty arṇave । sa u jyeṣṭhavaro abhavat ।। devā devebhyaḥ paraḥ ।
sa vā adya mahad vadet ।। akṣitiś ca kṣitiś ca yā । vā ākūtim ā vahan ।। atho dhātā bṛhaspatiḥ ।
kaṃ te jyeṣṭham upāsata ।। -antar mahaty arṇave । taṃ te jyeṣṭham upāsata ।। kuto agnir ajāyata ।
dhātā sam abhavat kutaḥ ।। agner agnir ajāyata । dhātā dhātur ajāyata ।। devā devebhyaḥ paraḥ ।
kasmin te loka āsate ।। yām addhātaya id viduḥ । kasminn u sādhiśritā ।। kuto asthīny ābharat ।
ko māṃsaṃ kuta ābharat ।। māṃsaṃ majjānam ābharat । kaṃ lokam anu prāviśat ।। ye saṃbhāraiḥ samabharan ।
devāḥ puruṣam āviśan ।। jihvāṃ grīvāś ca kīkasāḥ । kas tat sam adadhād ṛṣiḥ ।। śroṇī hastāv atho mukham ।
saṃdhā sam adadhān mahī ।। saṃdhayā saṃhitaṃ mahat । ko asmin varṇam ābharat ।। tad u jānād vadhūḥ satī ।
sāsmin varṇam ābharat ।। pitā tvaṣṭur ya uttaraḥ । devāḥ puruṣam āviśan ।। pāpmāno nāma devatāḥ ।
śarīram anu prāviśan ।। satyaṃ yajño yaśo mahaḥ । śarīram anu prāviśan ।। rātayo arātayaś ca yāḥ ।
śarīram anu prāviśan ।। yaś ca hanteti neti ca । -aśraddhā cānu prāviśan ।। yac cānyad upadeśyam ।
ṛcaḥ sāmātho yajuḥ ।। abhīmodamudaś ca ye । śarīram anu prāviśan ।। -abhīlāpalapaś ca ye ।
āyujaḥ prayujo yujaḥ ।। akṣitiś ca kṣitiś ca yā । śarīrena ta īyante ।। saṃśiṣo viśiṣaś ca yāḥ ।
śarīram anu prāviśan ।। -īḍāśīḥ sūnṛterā । ṛtarīrṣyāyudho mṛdhaḥ ।। tvaraṇāḥ kṛpaṇāś ca yāḥ ।
bībhatsur asādhayan ।। tad aṣṭāpo asādayan । devāḥ puruṣam āviśan ।। yā virāḍ brahmaṇā saha ।
charīre adhi prajāpatiḥ ।। puruṣasya vi bhejire । devāḥ prāyacchann agnaye ।। idaṃ brahmeti manyate ।
śarīre adhi samāhitāḥ ।। pitā lokām̐ akalpayat । yathāṅgam anu prāviśan ।। sarve devā anu prāviśan ।
taṃ lokam aparājitam ।। sarve devā anu prāviśan । charīraṃ bahudhā hitam ।। anuvāka ।।
brahmaudanaṃ pacati putrakāmā । manthantu prajayā saheha ।। adroghāvitā vācam accha । yena devā asahanta śatrūn ।।
brahmaudanāya paktave jātavedaḥ । rayiṃ sarvavīraṃ ni yaccha ।। viśvān devān yajñiyām̐ eha vakṣaḥ । svargaṃ lokam adhi rohayainam ।।
pitṝṇām uta martyānām । taṃ vo yo devānāṃ sā imaṃ pārayāti ।। nīco nyubja dviṣataḥ sapatnān । sajātāṃs te balihṛtaḥ kṛṇotu ।।
ud ubjainaṃ mahate vīryāya । svargo loka iti yaṃ vadanti ।। pṛthivī devī sumanasyamānā । adhi gacchema sukṛtām ulokam ।।
aṃśūn yajamānāya sādhu । ūrdhvāṃ prajām uddharanty ud ūha ।। ā te devā yajñiyā yajñam aguḥ । tās te samṛddhīr iha rādhāyāmi ।।
vi vicyadhvaṃ yajñiyāsas tuṣaiḥ । -adhaspadaṃ dviṣatas pādayema ।। gṛhṇātu tvām aditiḥ śūraputrā । asmai rayiṃ sarvavīraṃ ni yaccha ।।
apāṃ tvā goṣṭho adhy arukṣad bharāya । asan vibhājya dhīrītarā jihītāt ।। ut tiṣṭha nāri tavasaṃ rabhasva । -agan yajñaḥ prati kumbhaṃ gṛbhāya ।।
ṛṣipraśiṣṭāpa ā haraitāḥ । ugraḥ paśumad vīravid vo astu ।। chucis tapiṣṭhas tapasā tapainam । imaṃ tapiṣṭhā ṛtubhis tapantu ।।
āpaś carum iva sarpantu śubhrāḥ । paktaudanasya sukṛtām etu lokam ।। somasyāṃśavas taṇḍulā yajñiyā ime । carur imaṃ paktvā sukṛtām etu lokam ।।
pratyaṅ enaṃ devatābhiḥ sahaidhi । ādityo devaḥ paramaṃ vyoma ।। sahasrapṛṣṭhaḥ sukṛtasya loke । -ahaṃ paktvā pañcadaśas te asmi ।।
brahmaudano devayānaḥ svargaḥ । -enaṃ balihārāya mṛḍatāṃ mahyam eva ।। nudasva rakṣaḥ prataraṃ dhehy enam । -adhaspadaṃ dviṣataḥ pādayema ।।
brahmaudanasya nihitā vedir agre । tatraudanaṃ sādaya daivānām ।। saptarṣayo bhūtakṛto yām akṛṇvan । darvir vedyām adhy enaṃ cinotu ।।
ārṣeyās te mā riṣan prāśitāraḥ ।। subrāhmaṇā yatame tvopasīdān । brahmaudane suhavā johavīmi ।। brahmaṇāṃ hasteṣu pra pṛthak sādayāmi ।
indro marutvāṃs tad adād idaṃ me ।। pakvaṃ kṣetrāt kāmadughā ma eṣā । kṛṇve panthāṃ pitṛṣu yaḥ svargaḥ ।। paraḥ kambūkān upa mṛḍhy etān ।
atho vidma nirṛter bhāgadheyam ।। svargaṃ lokam adhi rohayainam । yena rohāt param āpadya yad vayaḥ ।। ājyāya lokaṃ kṛṇuhi prajānan ।
kṛṇve panthāṃ pitṛṣu yaḥ svargaḥ ।। brāhmaṇā yatame tvopasīdān । ārṣeyās te mā riṣan prāśitāraḥ ।। nānārṣeyāṇām apy asty atra ।
viśve devā abhi rakṣantu pakvam ।। pumāṃsaṃ dhenuṃ sadanaṃ rayīṇām । rāyaś ca poṣam upa tvā sadema ।। vṛṣabho asi svarga ṛṣīn ārṣeyān gaccha ।
sukṛtāṃ loke sīda tan nau saṃkṛtam ।। agne pathaḥ kalpaya devayānān । nāke tiṣṭhantam adhi saptaraśmau ।। brahmaudanaṃ paktvā sukṛtasya lokam ।
sa nas taṃ dhehi sukṛtām uloke ।। śatadhāram apakṣudham । yatra ṛṣayaḥ prathamajāḥ purāṇāḥ ।। dakṣiṇāyai tvā ।।
pratīcyai tvā ।। udīcyai tvā ।। dhruvāyai tvā ।। ūrdhvāyai tvā ।।
dive tvā ।। antarikṣāya tvā ।। pṛthivyai tvā ।। paśubhyas tvā ।।
manuṣyebhyas tvā ।।ṛṣibhyas tvā ।।aṅgirobhyas tvā ।।āṅgirasebhyas tvā ।।atharvabhyas tvā ।।ātharvaṇebhyas tvā ।।vanaspatibhyas tvā ।।vānaspatyebhyas tvā ।। vīrudbhyas tvā ।।ṛtubhyas tvā ।।lokebhyas tvā ।।lokānāṃ tvādhyakṣebhyaḥ ।।daivyebhyas tvā ।। śatadhāram apakṣudham । yatra ṛṣayaḥ prathamajāḥ purāṇāḥ ।।
na te śiṣṇaṃ pra dahāj jātavedāḥ । bhavāt te straiṇam apy apsarāsu ।। antarikṣam idaṃ mahat । yas tvā pacaty odana ।।
sapta puṣkariṇīr uta । yas tvā pacaty odana ।। devā hotāra ṛtvijaḥ । satyenāgre samairayan ।।
ṛṣayaḥ sādhyāś ca ye । śraddhayāgre sam airayan ।। brāhmaṇaṃ ca na hiṃsati । yamo rājābhi rakṣati ।।
dyumātraṃ devasaṃhitam । taṃ te brahmābhi rakṣatu ।। dyauḥ pṛṣṭhaṃ diśaḥ pārśve । ṛtavo dantāḥ pavamānaḥ prāṇo aṅgiraso rūpam ।।
anuvāka ।। lokam api gacchatu prajānan । ajo nākam ā kramatāṃ tṛtīyam ।। śuddhaiḥ śaphair ā kramatāṃ prajānan ।
tṛtīye nāke adhi vi kramasva ।। yathāparv asinā māti maṃsthāḥ । sukṛtāṃ madhye adhi vi śrayemam ।। ā siñcodakam ava dhehy enam ।
śṛto gacchatu sukṛtāṃ yatra lokaḥ ।। taptāc caror adhi nākaṃ tṛtīyam । jyotiṣmān gaccha sukṛtāṃ yatra lokaḥ ।। -ākraṃsyamānaḥ pañca jyotīm̐ṣi ।
jyotiṣmantam abhi lokaṃ jayāsmai ।। ajaṃ brahmaṇe jīyatā deyam āhuḥ । asmiṃl loke śraddadhānena dattaḥ ।। pañcaudanaṃ brahmaṇe ajaṃ dadāti ।
pañcaudano brahmaṇe dīyamānaḥ ।। ajo nākam ā kramatāṃ tṛtīyam । sa jyotiṣā tamo apa hanti dūram ।। śarabho nu catto ati durgāṇi neṣataḥ ।
viśvarūpā kāmadughāsy ekā ।। pañcaudanaṃ brahmaṇe ajaṃ dadāti । śivo asmabhyaṃ pratigṛhīta edhi ।। sukṛtāṃ loke dadivāṃsaṃ dadhāti ।
sa dātāraṃ tṛptyā tarpayāsi ।। vipro viprasya sahaso vayodhāḥ । tad devā ṛtuśaḥ kalpayantu ।। dhiraṇyam api dakṣiṇām ।
ye divyā ye ca pārthivāḥ ।। somyā devīr ghṛtapṛṣṭhā madhuścutaḥ । nāke tiṣṭhāsy adhi saptaraśmau ।। pṛṣṭhāt pṛthivyā iti catasraḥ ।।
।। ।। ।। darvyod dhara pañcadhaudanam etam ।
udīcīṃ dhruvām ūrdhvāṃ diśam ā kramasva ।। dakṣiṇāyāṃ diśi dakṣiṇaṃ dhehi pārśvam । udīcyāṃ diśy uttaraṃ dhehi pārśvam ।। diśi dhehi pājasyaṃ dhruvāyām ।
padbhiś caturbhiḥ prati tiṣṭha dikṣu ।। sarvair aṅgaiḥ saṃbhṛtaṃ viśvarūpam । padbhiś caturbhiḥ prati tiṣṭha dikṣu ।। sāntardeśāḥ prati gṛhṇantu tejasam ।
tābhyo juhomi haviṣā ghṛtena ।। yā vipruṣa odanānām ajasya । jānītān naḥ saṃgamane pathīnām ।। ajaḥ pañcaudano vy akramata ।
udaram antarikṣaṃ dyauḥ pṛṣṭhaṃ diśaḥ pārśve ।। satyaṃ ca rtaṃ ca cakṣuṣī । viśvaṃ rūpaṃ śraddhā prāṇo virāṭ śiraḥ ।। yad ajaḥ pañcaudanaḥ ।
ya evaṃ viduṣe ajaṃ pañcaudanaṃ dadāti ।। na majjño nir dhayet । -idaṃidaṃ pra veśayet ।। tenainaṃ saṃ gamayati ।
ya evaṃ viduṣe ajaṃ pañcaudanaṃ dadāti ।। imaṃ yajñaṃ yajñapatiś ca sūriḥ । -ariṣṭā vīrā yajamānasya sarve ।। pañca lokāḥ pañca rtavaḥ ।
ya evaṃ viduṣe ajaṃ pañcaudanaṃ dadāti ।। yad ajaḥ pañcaudanaḥ । ।। yo vā āyantam ity ṛtuṃ veda ।
।। vai saṃyantam iti । saṃyatīm eva ।। vai bhavantam iti ।
bhavantīm eva ।। vā abhibhavantam iti । abhibhavantīm eva ।। vā udyantam iti ।
udyatīm eva ।। vai mūrdhānam iti । mūrdhnīm eva ।। yo vai sarvam ity ṛtuṃ veda ।
ya evaṃ viduṣe ajaṃ pañcaudanaṃ dadāti ।। brahmāstṛṇoti vedyām । samudrasyevākṣitāḥ ।। surā bhūtvopa tiṣṭhāt surāpām ।
ajo nāke tiṣṭhatu modamānaḥ ।। dyauś ca bhūmiś ca tiṣṭhataḥ । yat prāṇan nimiṣac ca yat ।। sahasrākṣaraṃ pra puro ni paścāt ।
yad asyārdhaṃ katamaḥ sa ketuḥ ।। pṛṣṭayo yuktā anusaṃvahanti । paraṃ nedīyo avaraṃ davīyaḥ ।। ṣaḍ yamā eka ekajaḥ ।
ya eṣām eka ekajaḥ ।। yasmin yaśo nihitaṃ viśvarūpam । ye asya gopā mahato babhūvuḥ ।। ny anyā arkam abhito 'viśanta ।
harito hariṇīr ā viveśa ।। trīṇi nabhyāni ka u tac ciketa । ṣaṣṭiś ca khīlā avicācalā ye ।। antavac cā samakte ।
vidvān bhūtaṃ yad u bhavyam asya ।। jaran nāma mahat padam । ejat prāṇan nimiṣac ca yat ।। kumbhenevodahāryam ।
na sarve manasā viduḥ ।। pūrṇād ūnam ud acyate । yatas tat pariṣicyate ।। adṛśyamāno bahudhā pra jāyate ।
yad asyārdhaṃ kim u taj jajāna ।। aprāṇat prāṇan nimiṣac ca tiṣṭhat । tat saṃbhūya bhavaty ekam eva ।। yā viśvato yujyate yota sarvataḥ ।
tāṃ tvā pṛcchāmi katamā nu sarcām ।। astaṃ yatra ca gacchati । tato nāpy eti kiṃ cana ।। -arvāṅ vi paśyati ।
yasmin jyeṣṭham adhi śritam ।। yābhyāṃ nirmathyate vasu । sa vidyād brāhmaṇaṃ mahat ।। so agre svar ābharat ।
sarvam ādatta bhojanam ।। atho annam adad bahu । upāsātai sanātanam ।। utādyāsat punar navaḥ ।
anyo anyasya rūpayoḥ ।। asaṃkhyeyaṃ svam asmin niviṣṭam । tasmād devo rocate sa etat ।। utaikaṃ naiva dṛśyate ।
devatā sā mama priyā ।। martyasyāmṛtā gṛhe । yaś cakāra tadāra saḥ ।। tvaṃ kumāry uta vā kumāraḥ ।
tvaṃ jāto bhavasi viśvatomukhaḥ ।। utaiṣa bhrātota vā pitaiṣaḥ । prathamo jātaḥ sa u garbhe antaḥ ।। viśvā bhūtāni paryābhṛtasya ।
sarvān antān gacchatu tiṣṭhann eva ।। vi cakramāṇau rajasasphātyantau । antarā pūrvam aparaṃ ca ketum ।। vedaṃ vidvāṃsam abhito vadanti ।
agniṃ dvitīyaṃ trivṛtaṃ ca haṃsam ।। dvādaśabhir agnibhiḥ । tasyām oṣadhayaḥ śritāḥ ।। anuṣṭubhā saṃbhṛtaṃ vāyum etam ।
manaḥ punātu salilasya pṛṣṭhe ।। sapta rakṣanti sadam apramādam । tatra jāgṛto asvapnajau satrasadau ca devau ।। anuvāka ।।
bhūtapatī paśupatī namo vām । mā no hiṃsiṣṭaṃ dvipado mā catuṣpadaḥ ।। ye ca kṛṣṇā aviṣyavaḥ । vayāṃsi te vighase mā vidanta ।।
yāś ca te bhava ropayaḥ । sahasrākṣāmartya ।। uttarād adharād uta । antarikṣāya te namaḥ ।।
yāni cakṣūṃṣi te bhava । pratīcīnāya te namaḥ ।। jihvāyā āsyāya ca । dadbhyo gandhāya te namaḥ ।।
sahasrākṣeṇa vājinā । tena mā sam arāmahi ।। āpa ivāgniḥ pari vṛṇaktu no bhavaḥ । mā no abhi maṃsta namo astv asmai ।।
daśa kṛtvaḥ paśupate namas te । gāvo aśvāḥ puruṣā ād ajāvayaḥ ।। tavedam ugrorv antarikṣam । yad ejad adhi bhūmyām ।।
yasminn imā viśvā bhūtāny antaḥ । paraḥ kroṣṭāro abhibhāḥ śvānaḥ । paro yantv agharudo vikeśyaḥ ।। sahasraghni śatavadhaṃ śikhaṇḍin ।
tasmai namo yatamasyāṃ diśītaḥ ।। tvām ugra nicikīrṣati । taṃ viddhasya padanīr iva ।। ubhā ugrau carato vīryāya ।
tābhyāṃ namo bhavamatyāya kṛṇmaḥ ।। namo astu parāyate । āsīnāyota te namaḥ ।। namo rātryā namo divā ।
-ubhābhyām akaraṃ namaḥ ।। rudram asyantaṃ bahudhā vipaścitam । mopārāma jihvayeyamānam ।। bhīmaṃ rathaṃ keśinaḥ pādayantam ।
pūrve pratīmo namo astv asmai ।। mā naḥ krudhaḥ paśupate namas te । anyatrāsmad divyāṃ śākhāṃ vi dhūnu ।। pari ṇo vṛṅdhi mā krudha ।
mā tvayā sam arāmahi ।। mā gṛdho no ajāviṣu । piyārūṇāṃ prajāṃ jahi ।। -aśvasyeva vṛṣaṇaḥ kranda eti ।
namo astv asmai ।। ayajvanaḥ pramṛṇan devapīyūn । tasmai namo daśabhiḥ śakvarībhiḥ ।। vayāṃsi śakunāḥ patatriṇaḥ ।
tubhyaṃ kṣaranti divyā āpo vṛdhe ।। rajasā yebhyo asyasi । sarvāṃ pari paśyasi bhūmim ।। mā no rudra takmanā na viṣeṇa ।
-anyatrāsmad vidyutāṃ pātayaitām ।। bhava ā papra urv antarikṣam । tasya na prāpad ducchunā kā caneha ।। paśūnāṃ hi paśupatir babhūtha ।
catuṣpade dvipade asya mṛḍa ।। mā naḥ kṣiyantam uta mā no akṣitaḥ । svāṃ tanvaṃ rudra mā rīriṣo naḥ ।। asaṃsūktagirebhyaḥ ।
idaṃ mahāsyebhyaḥ śvabhyo akaraṃ namaḥ ।। namas te keśinībhyaḥ । namo namasvatībhyaḥ ।। jātāyā uta te namaḥ ।
rūpāyāghnye te namaḥ ।। sapta vidyāt parāvataḥ । sa vaśāṃ prati gṛhṇīyāt ।। sapta veda parāvataḥ ।
somaṃ cāsyāṃ vicakṣaṇam ।। yayāpo gupitā imāḥ । brahmaṇācchā vadāmasi ।। śataṃ goptāro adhi pṛṣṭhe asyāḥ ।
te vaśāṃ vidur ekadhā ।। svadhāprāṇā mahīlukā । devām̐ apyeti brahmaṇā ।। anu somo vaśe tvā ।
vidyutas te stanā vaśe ।। urvarā aparā vaśe । annaṃ kṣīraṃ vaśe tvam ।। -upatiṣṭha ṛtāvari ।
somaṃ tvāpāyayad vaśe ।। āt tva ṛṣabho ahvayat । kṣīraṃ kruddho abharad vaśe ।। kṣīraṃ te abharad vaśe ।
triṣu pātreṣu rakṣati ।। ā devy abharad vaśā । barhiṣy āsta hiraṇyaye ।। sam u sarveṇa padvatā ।
ṛcaḥ sāmāni bibhratī ।। sam u sarveṇa cakṣuṣā । gandharvaiḥ kalibhiḥ saha ।। sam u sarvaiḥ patatribhiḥ ।
bhadrā jyotīṃṣi bibhratī ।। vaśā deṣṭry atho svadhā । barhiṣy āsta hiraṇyaye ।। yad atiṣṭha ṛtāvari ।
-adhy askandad vaśe tvā ।। vaśā mātā svadhe tava । tataś cittam ajāyata ।। brahmaṇaḥ kakudād adhi ।
tato hotā ajāyata ।। -uṣṇihābhyo balaṃ tava । stanebhyo raśmayo vaśe ।। sakthibhyāṃ ca vaśe tava ।
udarād adhi vīrudhaḥ ।। -anu prāviśathā vaśe । sa hi netram avet tava ।। jāyamānād asūsvaḥ ।
brahmaṇā kl̥pta uta bandhur asyāḥ ।। yo asyā eka id vaśī । tarasāṃ cakṣur abhavad vaśā ।। vaśā yajñam adhārayat ।
odano brahmaṇā saha ।। vaśāṃ mṛtyum upāsate । manuṣyā asurāḥ pitara ṛṣayaḥ ।। ya evaṃ vidyāt sa vaśāṃ prati gṛhṇīyāt ।
duhe dātre anapasphuran ।। -antar didyaty āsani । sa vaśā duṣpratigrahā ।। yajñas turīyaṃ paśavas turīyam ।
ya evaṃ vidyāt sa vaśāṃ prati gṛhṇīyāt ।। vaśā viṣṇuḥ prajāpatiḥ । sādhyā vasavaś ca ye ।। sādhyā vasavaś ca ye ।
payo asyā upāsate ।। ghṛtam eka upāsate । te gatās tridivaṃ divaḥ ।। sarvāṃl lokān sam aśnute ।
api brahmātho tapaḥ ।। vaśāṃ manuṣyā uta । yāvat sūryo vipaśyati ।। anuvāka ।।
yo vā ekaṃ brahmānuṣṭhyā vidyāt sa vā adya mahad vadet ।। ṛco yasyānūkyam ।। yajur hṛdayam ucyate ।। yad atithipatir atithīn pratipaśyati devayajanaṃ prekṣate ।।
yad udakaṃ yācaty apaḥ pra ṇayati । yā yajñā apaḥ praṇīyante tā eva tāḥ ।। yat tarpaṇam āharanti yo agnīṣomīyaḥ paśur badhyate sa eva saḥ ।। yad āvasathān kalpayanti sadohavirdhānāny eva tat kalpayanti ।।
yad upastṛṇanti barhir eva tat ।। yat kaśipūpabarhaṇāny āharanti paridhaya eva te । yad upariśayanam āharanti svargam eva tena lokam ava rundhe ।। yad abhyañjanam āharanty ājyam eva tat ।
yad aśanakṛtaṃ hvayanti haviṣkṛtam eva tad u hvayanti । yad vrīhayo yad yavā nirupyante aṃśava eva te ny upyante ।। śūrpaṃ pavitraṃ tūṣā ṛjīṣaḥ । āpo abhiṣavaṇī yad droṇakalaśaḥ kumbhī ।।
idam eva kṛṣṇājinaṃ vāyavyāni pātrāṇi । yad āhāryāṇy avekṣata idaṃ bhūyā idām iti ।। prāṇam eva tena varṣīyāṃsaṃ kṛṇute । kāmaṃ hi pṛṣṭo yācati ।।
yad udakam abhiṣiñcaty apa eva tenāva rundhe । yad upaharati havīṃṣy ā sādayati ।। teṣām āsannānām atithir ātmani juhoti । srukkāreṇa vaṣatkāreṇa srucā hastena prāṇe yūpe ।।
na mīmāṃsitasya na mīmāṃsyamānasya ।। yasyānnam aśnanti ।। yasyānnaṃ nāśnanti ।। prajāpater vā eṣa vikrāntam anuvikrame ya upaharanti ।।
prajāpatyo vā etasyaiva yajño vitato ya upaharati ।। āhṛtayajñakratur vitatādhavaro ya upaharati ।। yo veśmani sa gārhapatyaḥ ।। yaḥ pūrvo atither aśnāti ।।
।। yaḥ pūrvo atither aśnāti ।। eṣa vā atithir yac chrotriyaḥ ।। tasmāt pūrvo nāśnīyād aśitāvaty aśnīyāt tad vratam ।।
yajñasyāvicchedāya yajñasya guptaye yajñasya sātmatvāya ।। yāvad agniṣṭomea samṛddheneṣṭvāvarundhe tāvad enenāva rundhe ।। yāvat sāhnena samṛddhena ।। yāvad atirātreṇa samṛddhena ।।
yāvad dvādaśāhnena samṛddheneṣṭvāvarundhe tāvad enenāva rundhe ।। prajānāṃ prajananāya jyog jīvati sarvam āyur eti na punar ā jarasaḥ pramīyate ya evaṃ veda ।। bṛhaspatir ūrjayodgāyati tvaṣṭā puṣṭyā prati harati viśve devā nidhanam । nidhanaṃ bhūtyāḥ prajāyāḥ paśūnāṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda ।।
madhyandina udgāyaty aparāhṇaḥ prati haraty astaṃyan nidhanam । ।। stanayann udgāyati varṣan prati haraty udgṛhṇan nidhanam । ।।
udakaṃ yācaty udgāyaty upa harati prati haraty ucchiṣṭaṃ nidhanam । nidhanaṃ bhūtyāḥ prajāyāḥ paśūnāṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda ।। svargaṃ lokaṃ gamayanti yad atithayaḥ ।। yat pratiśṛṇoti praty ā śrāvayati ।।
teṣāṃ naikaś canāhotā ।। prātaḥsavanam eva tat ।। mādhyaṃdinam eva tat savanam ।। tṛtīyasavanam eva tat ।।
avabhṛtham eva tad upāvaiti ।। yad anutiṣṭhaty udavasyaty eva tat ।। upahūtas tasmin yat pṛthivyāṃ viśvarūpam । svargaloko bhavati ya evaṃ veda ।।
upahūtas tasmin yad antarikṣe viśvarūpam । ।। upahūtas tasmin yad divi viśvarūpam । ।।
upahūtas tasmin yad deveṣu viśvarūpam । ।। upahūtas tasmin yal lokeṣu viśvarūpam । svargaloko bhavati ya evaṃ veda ।।
yajñāya ca devebhyaś cā vṛścate ।। yamāya ca pitṛbhyaś cā vṛścate ।। varuṇāyāpsuṣada ā vṛścate ।। somāya ca rājñe saptaṛṣibhyaś cāvṛścate ।।
vāyave cāntarikṣāya cā vṛścate ।। dive cādityāya cāvṛścate ।। yaṃ kāmayeta pāpīyān ātmanā prajayā paśubhir gṛhair dhanena syād iti । tasyaivaṃ nirupyaivam evānu nirvapet ।
idamidaṃ kuryāt sā prāyaścītiḥ ।। yaṃ kāmayeta na vasīyān na śreyān ātmanā prajayā paśubhir gṛhair dhanena syād iti । tasyaivaṃ nirupayaivam evānu nirvapet । idamidaṃ kuryāt sa prāyaścittiḥ ।।
yaṃ kāmayeta vasīyāñ chreyān ātmanā prajayā paśubhir gṛhair dhanena syād iti । tasyaivaṃ nirupyaivam evānu nirvapet । idamidaṃ kuryāt sā prāyaścittiḥ ।। samāṃsamāmasya varaḥ pramāyuko bhavati ।।
pitṛdevatyaṃ karoti ।। gṛhāṇāṃ ca paśūnāṃ ca payo vi ṣyandate ।। gṛhāṇāṃ ca paśūnāṃ ca payo apa siñcati ।। gṛhapatir mriyate ।।
gṛhapatnī mriyate ।। sarvajyānir dātā ca pratigṛhītā ca jīyete ।। yajñāya ca devebhyaś cā vṛścate ।। yamāya ca pitṛbhyaś cā vṛścate ।।
varuṇāyāpsuṣada ā vṛścate ।। somāya ca rājñe saptaṛṣibhyaś cā vṛścate ।। diśodiśa evainaṃ bhayam ā gacchati ।। yajñāya ca devebhyaś cā vṛścate ।।
yamāya ca pitṛbhyaś cā vṛścate ।। akṛtapūrvaṃ karoti ।। somāya ca rājñe saptaṛṣibhyaś cā vṛścate ।। arśaḥ pratigrahītur mukhe jāyate ।।
yamāya ca pitṛbhyaś cā vṛścate ।। pratīcī pratigrahītāraṃ śaravya rcchati ।। somāya ca rājñe saptaṛṣibhyaś cā vṛścate ।। ādityānām eva priyaṃ dhāmopaiti ।
ādityānāṃ tvā priyeṇa dhāmnā prāśnāmīty enaṃ prāśnīyāt । ādityebhyaś cā vṛścate ।। viśveṣām eva devānāṃ priyaṃ । viśveṣāṃ tvā devānāṃ priyeṇa dhāmnā ।
viśvebhyo devebhyaś cā vṛścate ।। marutām eva priyaṃ । marutāṃ tvā priyeṇa । marudbhyaś cā vṛścate ।।
agner eva । agnes tvā priyeṇa । agnaye cā vṛścate ।। mitrāvaruṇayor eva ।
mitrāvaruṇayos tvā priyeṇa । mitrāvaruṇābhyāṃ cā vṛścate ।। -indrasyaiva । indrasya tvā ।
-indrāya cā vṛścate ।। pitṝṇām eva । pitṝṇāṃ tvā । pitṛbhyaś cā vṛścate ।।
apām eva । apāṃ tvā priyeṇa । adbhyaś cā vṛścate ।। diśām eva ।
diśāṃ tvā । [see digbhyaś cā vṛścate ।। prajāpater eva । prajāpateṣ ṭvā ।
prajāpataye cā vṛścate ।। ūrdhvanabhasa eva priyaṃ dhāmopaiti । ūrdhvanabhasas tvā priyeṇa dhāmnā prāśnāmīty enaṃ prāśnīyāt । ūrdhvanabhase cā vṛścate ।।
pratigrahītā bhavati ।। pratigrahītāraṃ hanti ।। pratigrahītāraṃ hanti ।। pratigrahītāraṃ hanti ।।
yad udakam upasicya prathamaṃ prāśnāti tat samṛddham । jyog jīvati sarvam āyur eti na purā jarasaḥ pramīyate ya evaṃ veda ।। yat prāśiṣyan purastād atimṛśati । evaṃ cainaṃ prāśnantam upadraṣṭā gṛhṇāti ।।
yat prāśiṣyan dakṣiṇataḥ pramṛśati । dakṣiṇā pratigrahītuḥ ।। evaṃ cainaṃ prāśnantam upadraṣṭā gṛhṇāti ।। yat prāśiṣyan paścāt prāñcam abhimṛśati ।
jayaty odanam odanaloko bhavati ya evaṃ veda ।। anuvāka ।। -indrasya nṛmṇaṃ sthendrasya śukraṃ sthendrasya vīryaṃ stha । yuktā ma āpa stha ।।
yogāya kṣatrayogair vaḥ ।। yogāya brahmayogair vaḥ ।। yogāyānnayogair vaḥ ।। -indrasya nṛmṇaṃ sthendrasya śukraṃ sthendrasya vīryaṃ stha ।
yuktā ma āpa stha ।। agner bhāga stha । apāṃ śukraṃ devīr āpo varco asmāsu dhatta । prajāpater vo dhāmnāsmai lokāya sādaye ।।
indrasya bhāga stha । ।। somasya bhāga stha । ।।
varuṇasya bhāga stha । ।। yamasya bhāga stha । ।।
pitṝṇāṃ bhāga stha । ।। bṛhaspater bhāga stha । ।।
prajāpater bhāga stha । ।। devasya savitur bhāga stha । apāṃ śukraṃ devīr āpo varco asmāsu dhatta ।
prajāpater vo dhāmnāsmai lokāya sādaye ।। yo va āpo apāṃ bhāgo apsv antar yajuṣyo devayajanaḥ । idaṃ tam ati sṛjāmi taṃ mābhy ava nikṣi । yo asmān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ ।
taṃ vadheyaṃ taṃ stṛṣīyānena brahmaṇānena karmaṇānayā menyā ।। apām ūrmir apsv antar yajuṣyaḥ ।। apāṃ vegaḥ ।। apāṃ binduḥ ।।
apāṃ garbhaḥ ।। apāṃ vatsaḥ ।। apāṃ vṛṣabhaḥ ।। apām aśmā pṛśnir divyo apsv antar yajuṣyaḥ ।।
yo va āpo apāṃ hiraṇyagarbho apsv antar yajuṣyo devayajanaḥ । idaṃ tam ati sṛjāmi taṃ mābhy ava nikṣi । tena tam ।। ye va āpo apām agnayo apsv antar yajuṣyā devayajanāḥ ।
idaṃ tān ati sṛjāmi tān mābhy ava nikṣi । yo asmān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ । taṃ vadheyaṃ taṃ stviṣīyānena brahmaṇānena karmaṇānayā menyā ।। anṛtaṃ kiṃ codima ।
duritāt pāntu viśvataḥ ।। ariprā āpo apa ripram asmat । pra duṣvapnyaṃ pra malaṃ vahantu ।। svāṃ yonim apītana ।
mā ca naḥ kiṃ canāmamat ।। pṛthivīsaṃśito agnitejāḥ । yo asmān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ । apāṅ apanuttaḥ sapatnaḥ ।।
-antarikṣasaṃśito vāyutejāḥ । yo asmān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ । sahajān sapatnān ।। dyusaṃśitaḥ sūryatejāḥ ।
yo asmān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ । aparajān sapatnān ।। diksaṃśito vātatejāḥ । digbhyas tam ।।
-āśāsaṃsito manastejāḥ । āśābhyas tam ।। -apsaṃsito varuṇatejāḥ । adbhyas tam ।।
ṛksaṃśitaḥ sāmatejāḥ । ṛgbhyas tam ।। yajñasaṃśito brahmatejāḥ । yajñāt tam ।।
-oṣadhīsaṃśitaḥ somatejāḥ । oṣadhībhyas tam ।। kṛṣisaṃśitaḥ puruṣatejāḥ । kṛṣyās tam ।।
prāṇasaṃśito annatejāḥ । yo asmān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ ।। abhy aṣṭhāṃ viśvāḥ pṛtanā arātīḥ । -idam enam adhamaṃ tamo gamayāmi ।।
sūryasyāvṛtam anv āvarte dakṣiṇām anv āvṛtam । brāhmaṇān abhi paryāvarte । te me brāhmaṇavarcasam ।। ākṣiyati pṛthivīm anu ।
saṃprayaccha prajāpate । taṃ vadhai stṛṇavāmahi ।। brahmaṇāpīpadāma tam । mṛtyus taṃ samadhād abhi ।।
samid devī sahīyasī । so amum āmuṣyāyaṇam amuṣyāḥ putram anne prāṇe badhāna ।। caturbhṛṣṭiṃ śīrṣabhidyāya vidvān । tan me devā hy anu jānantu viśve ।।
upa prekṣāmahe vayam । -āyuṣmantaḥ sumedhasaḥ ।। tasyā jātāyā abibhet sarvam । iyam evedaṃ bhaviṣyati na vayam iti ।।
sod akrāmat sā dakṣiṇāgnau ny akrāmat । yajñarto vāsateyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda ।। sā gārhapatye ny akrāmat । gṛhamedhī gṛhapatir bhavati ।।
sāhavanīye ny akrāmat । yanty asya devā devahūtiṃ priyo devānāṃ bhavati ।। sā sabhāyāṃ ni । yanty asya sabhāṃ sabhyo bhavati ।।
sā samitau ni । yanty asya samitiṃ sāmityo bhavati ।। sāmantraṇe ny akrāmat । yanty asyāmantraṇam āmantraṇīyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda ।।
-imām upa hvayāmahā iti tām upahvāyanta । ūrja ehi svadha ehi sūnṛta ehīrāvaty ehīti । tasyā agnir vatsa āsīd gāyatry abhidhāny abhram ūdhaḥ ।। yajñāyajñiyaṃ ca vāmadevyaṃ ca dvau ।
apo vāmadevyaṃ yajñaṃ yajñāyajñiyam ।। ete vai virājaḥ kāmadugha stanāḥ । kāmaṃkāmaṃ virājaṃ duhe ya evaṃ veda ।। sā saṃvatsare sam abhavat ।
vṛścyanty asyāpriyaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ ya ।। sā māse sam abhavat । svadhāvān pitṛṣu bhavati pra pitṛyāṇaṃ panthāṃ jānāti yaḥ ।। sārdhamāse sam abhavat ।
juhoty agnihotraṃ pra devayānaṃ panthāṃ jānāti yaḥ ।। sā sadyaḥ sam abhavat । upāsya gṛhe haranti yaḥ ।। tām asurā upāhvayanta māya ehīti ।
tasyā virocanaḥ prāhrādur vatsa āsīd ayaspātraṃ pātram । tāṃ dvimūrdhārtviyo adhok tāṃ māyām adhok । upajīvanīyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda ।। tāṃ pitara upāhvayanta svadha ehīti ।
tasyā yamo vaivasvato vatsa āsīd rajatapātraṃ pātram । tām antako mārtayo adhok tāṃ svadhām adhok । tāṃ svadhāṃ pitara upa ।। tāṃ manuṣyā upāhvayanterāvaty ehīti ।
tasyā manur vaivasvato vatsa āsīt pṛthivīpātraṃ pātram । tāṃ pṛthur vainyo adhok tāṃ kṛṣiṃ ca sasyaṃ cādhok । tāṃ kṛṣiṃ ca sasyaṃ ca manuṣya upa ।। tāṃ devā upāhvayantorja ehīti ।
tasyā indro vatsa āsīd dārupātraṃ pātram । tāṃ savitādhok tām ūrjam adhok । tām ūrjaṃ devā upa ।। tāṃ sapta ṛṣaya upāhvayanta brahmaṇvaty ehīti ।
tasyāḥ somo vatsa āsīc chandaḥpātraṃ pātram । tāṃ bṛhaspatir āṅgiraso adhok tāṃ brahma ca tapaś cādhok । tad brahma ca tapaś ca sapta ṛṣaya upa ।। tāṃ gandharvāpsarasa upāhvayanta puṇyagandha ehīti ।
tasyāś citrarathaḥ sauryavarcaso vatsa āsīt puṣkaraparṇaṃ pātram । tāṃ vasuruciḥ sauryavarcaso adhok tāṃ puṇyaṃ gandham adhok । taṃ puṇyaṃ gandhaṃ gandharvāpsarasā upa ।। tāṃ puṇyajanā upāhvayanta tirodha ehīti ।
tasyāḥ kubero vaiśravaṇo vatsa āsīd āmapātraṃ pātram । tāṃ rajatanābhiḥ kāberako adhok tāṃ tirodhām adhok । tāṃ tirodhāṃ puṇyajanā upa ।। tāṃ sarpā upāhvayanta viṣavaty ehīti ।
tasyās takṣako vaiśāleyo vatsa āsīd alābupātraṃ pātram । tāṃ dhṛtarāṣṭra airāvato adhok tāṃ viṣam adhok । upajīvanīyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda ।। manasā tvā pratyāhanmīty enaṃ pratyāhanyāt ।
na ca pratyāhanti viṣam anu prasicyate । viṣam asyāpriyaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ hanti ya evaṃ veda ।। anuvāka ।। sapatneṣu vajram arpayaitam ।
bhrātṛvyaghnī yajamānāya gātuḥ ।। barhir lomāni yāni te । grāvā tvaiṣo adhi nṛtyatu ।। jihvā saṃ mārṣṭv aghnye ।
divaṃ prehi śataudane ।। kāmapreṇa sa kalpate । sarve yanti yathāyatham ।। paktāro ye ca te janāḥ ।
maibhyo bhaiṣīḥ śataudane ।। yatrādas tridivaṃ divaḥ । yo dadāti śataudanām ।। yeṣu devāḥ samāsate ।
yo dadāti śataudanām ।। uttarān marutas tvā । sātirātram agniṣṭomam ati drava ।। rudrā aṅgirasas tvā ।
sātirātram agniṣṭomam ati drava ।। ādityān maruto diśaḥ । yo dadāti śataudanām ।। devān devī gamiṣyati ।
divaṃ prehi śataudane ।। ye ceme bhūmyām adhi । kṣīraṃ sarpir atho madhu ।। yau karṇau yau ca te akṣyau ।
kṣīraṃ sarpir atho madhu ।। ye dantā ye ca te hanū । ।। purītat sahakaṇṭhikā ।
।। āntrāṇi yāś ca te gudāḥ । ।। yau kukṣī yac ca ta udaram ।
।। yan māṃsaṃ yac ca lohitam । ।। doṣaṇī yā ca te kakut ।
।। yāḥ pṛṣṭīr yāś ca parśavaḥ । ।। ye śroṇī yā ca te bhasat ।
।। yad ūdho ye ca te stanāḥ । ।। ṛtsarā ye ca te śaphāḥ ।
।। yāni lomāny aghnye । kṣīraṃ sarpir atho madhu ।। ayaṃ sarpir ayaṃ madhu ।
duhāṃ devi śataudane ।। ājyenābhighāritau । sā dātāraṃ divaṃ vaha ।। ye vā śūrpe taṇḍulāḥ kaṇāḥ ।
-agniṣ ṭad dhotā suhutaṃ kṛṇotu ।। brahmaṇāṃ hasteṣu prapṛthak sādayāmi । vayaṃ syāma patayo rayīṇām ।। agnir lalāṭaṃ yamaḥ kṛkāṭaṃ somo rājā mastiṣkaḥ ।
dyaur uttarā hanuḥ pṛthivy adharā ।। maruto dantāḥ pavamānaḥ prāṇaḥ । kṛṣṇadraṃ vidharaṇī vikeśyaḥ ।। gharmo vahaḥ śyenaḥ kroḍo antarikṣaṃ pājasyam ।
tvaṣṭā cāryamā ca doṣaṇī ।। mahādevo bāhū bṛhaspatiḥ kakud bṛhatīḥ kīkasāḥ । devānāṃ patnīḥ pṛṣṭaya upasadaḥ parśavaḥ ।। indrāṇī bhasad vātaḥ pucchaṃ pavamāno bālāḥ ।
dhātā ca savitā cāṣṭhīvantau ।। kuṣṭhikā aditiḥ śaphāḥ । harimā pittaṃ vrataṃ purītat ।। itarajanā ūbadhyaṃ rakṣāṃsi lohitam ।
krodho vṛkkau manyur āṇḍau prajā śepaḥ ।। stanayitnur ūdho varṣasya pataya stanāḥ । viśvavyacāś carmauṣadhayo lomāni nakṣatrāṇi rūpam ।। abhraṃ pīvo majjā nidhanam ।
nidhanaṃ bhūtyāḥ prajāyāḥ paśūnāṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda ।। pratyaṅ tiṣṭhan dhātodaṅ tiṣṭhan savitā । tṛṇāni prāptaḥ somo rājāvṛtta ānandaḥ । īkṣamāno mitre yujyamāno vaiśvadevo yuktaḥ prajāpatir vimuktaḥ sarvam ।
etad vai gorūpam । upainaṃ rūpavantaḥ paśavas tiṣṭhanti ya evaṃ veda ।। brahmaṇā vittarte śritā । yajñe pratiṣṭhitā loko nidhanam ।।
-ayaṃ brāhmaṇo adhipatiḥ । jinato brāhmaṇaṃ kṣatriyasya । apa krāmati sūnṛtā vīryaṃ puṇyā lakṣmīḥ ।। ojaś ca tejaś ca sahaś ca balaṃ ca ।।vāk cendriyaṃ ca śrīś ca dharmaś ca ।।brahma ca kṣatraṃ ca rāṣṭraṃ ca viśaś ca ।।tviṣiś ca yaśaś ca varcaś ca draviṇaṃ ca ।।āyuś ca rūpaṃ ca nāma ca kīrtiś ca ।।payaś ca rasaś cānnaṃ cānnādyaṃ ca ।।prāṇaś cāpānaś ca cakṣuś ca śrotraṃ ca ।।ṛtaṃ ca satyaṃ ceṣṭaṃ ca pūrtaṃ ca prajā paśavaś ca ।।tāni sarvāṇy apa krāmanti kṣatriyasya brahmagavīm ādadānasya ।।
sarvāṇy asyāṃ ghorāṇi sarve ca puruṣavadhāḥ ।। mṛtyoḥ paḍvīśa ā dyati । brahmajyasya kṣitir hi sā ।। durādharṣā vijānatā ।
hetiḥ śaphān utkhidantī ।। mṛtyur hiṅkṛṇvatī । brahmagavī brahmajyam ।। rājayakṣmo mehantī menir duhyamānā śīrṣaktir dugdhā ।
śaravyā mukhe apinahyamāne ।। -aghaviṣā nipatantī tamo nipatitā । anugacchantī prāṇān upa dāsayati brahmagavī brahmajyasya ।। devahetir hriyamāṇāmatir hitā nirṛtir nihitā ।
pāruṣyam avadhīyamānāprajastāvihitā ।। viṣaṃ prayasyantī takmā prayastā । mūlabarhaṇī paryākriyamāṇā kṣitiḥ paryākṛtā ।। aghaṃ pacyamānā parābhūtiḥ pakvā ।
sugudhriyamāṇāśīviṣa uddhṛtāsaṃjñā gandhena ।। abhūtir upahriyamāṇā parābhūtir upahṛtā । śimidā piśitā ।। ārtir aśyamānā vīkarto aśitā ।
aśitā lokāc chinatti brahmacārī brahmajyam asmāc cāmuṣmāc ca ।। asvagatā parihvṛtā । agniḥ kravyād bhūtvā brahmagavī brahmajyaṃ praviśyātti ।। chinatty asya pitṛbandhūn parā bhāvayati mātṛbandhūn ।
vivāhāṃ jñātīn sarvān api kṣāpayati brahmagavī kṣatriyasyāpunardīyamānā ।। aparāparaṇo bhavati kṣīyate । ya evaṃ viduṣo brāhmaṇasya kṣatriyo gām ādatte ।। gṛdhrāḥ kurvata ailavam ।
kurvāṇāḥ pāpam ailavam ।। gaṅgaṇaṃ kurvate vṛkāḥ । yat tad āsīd idaṃ nu tāt ।। api kṣāpaya kṣāpaya ।
brahmajyam upa dāsaya ।। oṣantī samoṣantī brahmaṇo vajraḥ ।। kṣurapavir mṛtyur bhūtvāpidhāvitaḥ । iṣṭaṃ pūrtaṃ cāśiṣaḥ ।।
loke amuṣmin pra yacchasi । aghnye padavīr bhava brāhmaṇasyābhiśastyā ।। meniḥ śaravyā bhavāghād aghaviṣā bhava । agnhye pra śiro jahi brahmajyasya kṛtāgasaḥ ।।
devapīyum arādhasam । kṛnta pra kṛnta piṃśa pra piṃśauṣa sam oṣa daha pra daha । ā mūlād anu saṃdaha ।। saktaṃ keśeṣu nihitaṃ lalāṭe ।
apāmārgo apa lumpatu ।। karṇayor akṣṇor hitam । ।। daurbhāgyaṃ vācy oṣṭhayoḥ ।
।। jihvāyāṃ chubuke hitam । ।। daurbhāgyaṃ prāṇa āhitam ।
।। kaṇṭhe klomasu viṣṭhitam । ।। daurbhāgyaṃ kīkasāsv anūkye ।
।। aṃsayor upapakṣayoḥ । ।। aratnyoḥ kalkuṣīr anu ।
।। pāṇyor aṅgulīr anu । ।। jaghane sphijor hitam ।
।। pārśvayo stanayor hitam । ।। nābhyāṃ vakṣaṇā anu ।
।। yad vā yakani vṛkkayoḥ । ।। daurbhāgyam udare hitam ।
।। vaniṣṭhau plāśāv āhitam । ।। yad vā yāśuṣu muṣkayoḥ ।
।। avacālūśayor hitam । ।। ūrvor jānunor hitam ।
।। sthūrayoḥ pārṣṇyor hitam । ।। pādayor aṅgulīr anu ।
।। māṃse asthiṣu majjasu । ।। yad vā lomasu viṣṭhitam ।
।। prahāyām adhidevane । ।। kṛṣyām aśaner hitam ।
।। -atho yā te aputratā । ।। atho yā te apacitā ।
।। atho yā te apaśutā । apāmārgo apa lumpatu ।। devebhyaḥ kilbiṣaṃ yad babhūva ।
punātu mā śatadhāraṃ pavitram ।। kṛṣṇe cele sādayitvā pāpam । sūryaṃ jyotir abhy ehy agnim ।। mucyamāno aṃhasaḥ pāpmanaś ca ।
mā mā dabhan paṇayo yātudhānāḥ ।। aśastim adhy ātmanaḥ । teja ā dhīyatāṃ mayi । sarvam āyur aśīya ।।
anuvāka ।। brahma jajñānam ity ekā ।। divaṃ ca brahmāvādhūṣṭāmṛtena mṛtyum । brahmāsmad apa hantu śamalaṃ tamaś ca ।।
vitatāḥ paśyāmahai । -asurāṇām ayasmayī ।। ye tvā dipsanti divam utpatantam । divam ā roha sūrya ।।
pāśair aṅkino ye caranti । sahasrabhṛṣṭiḥ sapatnān pramṛṇan yāhi vajraḥ ।। ṛtena bhrājann amṛtaṃ vicaṣṭe । gharmo bhrājan divo antān pary eṣi vidyutā ।।
hiraṇyavarṇā amṛtā apsv antaḥ samudre । vaiśvānārasya hetiḥ pari ṇo vṛṇaktu ।। vyāghrā apsuṣado yatra bhīmāḥ । asapatnāḥ pradiśo me kṛṇotu ।।
divaṃ ca samiddho agnir divyas tapodhāḥ । apāṃ suparṇo diva eti pṛṣṭhe ।। gharmo bhrājan tejasā rocamāṇaḥ । ādityo dyām adhyarukṣad vipaścit ।।
divaṃ ca samiddho agnir divyas tapojāḥ । ṛtena bhrājann amṛtaṃ vaste atkī ।। śītarūre tanvāv asya bhīme । guhā kṛṇvānas tanvaḥ parācīḥ ।।
samārohanti bhuvanāni viśvā । sanād eva na chidyate sanābhiḥ ।। sahasradhāmānam anu tiṣṭhanty enam । brahmaṇādityas trivṛtā mukhena ।।
apsv antar amṛto gharma udyan । anādhṛṣṭās tanvaḥ sūryasya ।। ayodaṃṣṭrāya dviṣato api dadhmaḥ । sapatnān me dviṣato hantu sarvān ।।
śucānaḥ samidhā samiddhaḥ । brahmā tvā tapati brahmaṇā tejasā ca ।। na bibhide na bhidyate । tasya nāḍya ātatā vitatās tatā u tāḥ ।।
ya īṃ jajāna sa id asya bhartā । trīṇi jyotīṃṣi dadhate na pākaḥ ।। sa jāyamāno bahudhā pra jāyate । tasminn ārpitā bhuvanāni viśvā ।।
arā nābhāv iva śritāḥ । yatra tan māyayāhitam ।। māyayātihitaṃ guhā । sa vidyād brāhmaṇaṃ mahat ।।
ūrdhvas tiryaṅ viśa etu prajānan । sarvān antān gacchatu sadya eva ।। ādityo jātavedasā । varcasā saṃ sṛjāti mā ।।
asapatnāḥ pradiśo me kṛṇotu । hantu vaiśvānaro hariḥ ।। bhrātṛvyān dviṣato mama । udyan sūryaḥ pṛtanyataḥ ।।
bhrātṛvyān dviṣato vṛṣā । vi mṛdho hantu sūryaḥ ।। bhrājad ajasraṃ jyotir divam ā tatāna । sapatnān hantu mahātā vadhena ।।
hiraṇyavarṇo durudāpa āśuḥ । ādityo hantu raśmibhiḥ ।। ahorātre vidadhac chukra udyan । etu vaiśvānaro dahan ।।
udyann adya mitramaha ity ekā ।। ānandaṃ bhūtiṃ mahasaḥ pratiṣṭhām । amoghaṃ satyaṃ yaśa udyataṃ te ।। yasmin devāḥ saṃmanaso bhavanti ।
sa ācāryaṃ tapasā pipartu ।। kṛṇute garbham antaḥ । taṃ jātaṃ draṣṭum abhisaṃyanti devāḥ । gandharvā enam anu yanti sarve ।।
sarvān sa devāṃs tapasā piparti । -utāntarikṣaṃ samidhā pṛṇāti । śrameṇa lokāṃs tapasā piparti ।। gharmaṃ vasānas tapaso adhi tiṣṭhat ।
devāś ca sarve amṛtena sākam ।। kārṣṇaṃ vasāno dīkṣito dīrghaśmaśruḥ । lokān saṃrabhya muhur ācarikrat ।। parameṣṭhiṇaṃ virājam ।
indro bhūtvāsurāṃs tatarha ।। bhikṣāṃ jabhāra prathamo divaṃ ca । tayor ārpitā bhuvanāni viśvā ।। urvī gambhīre pṛthivīṃ divaṃ ca ।
tayor devāḥ sadhamādaṃ madanti ।। guhā nidhī nihitau brāhmaṇasya । tat kevalaṃ kṛṇute brahma vidvān ।। sameto nabhasī antareme ।
tān ā tiṣṭhati tapasā brahmacārī ।। bṛhacchepo anu bhūmau jabhāra । tena jīvanti pradiśaś catasraḥ ।। soma oṣadhayaḥ payaḥ ।
tair idaṃ svar ābharan ।। apsu samidham ā dadhāti । teṣām ājyaṃ puruṣo varṣam aśvaḥ ।। yadyad aicchat prajāpatau ।
svān mitro adhy ātmanaḥ ।। brahmacārī prajāpatiḥ । virāḍ indro abhavad vaśī ।। rājā rāṣṭraṃ vi rakṣate ।
brahmacāriṇam icchate ।। yuvānaṃ vindate patim । -aśvo ghāsaṃ jigīrṣati ।। devā mṛtyum apājayan ।
-amṛtaṃ svar ābharat ।। ahorātre vanaspatayaḥ । te jātā brahmacāriṇaḥ ।। āraṇyā grāmyā ca ye ।
te jātā brahmacāriṇaḥ ।। prāṇām̐ ātmasu bibhrati । brahmacāriṇy ābhṛtam ।। tasmin devā adhi viśve sametāḥ ।
pṛthivyāṃ bahu rocate ।। anabhyārūḍhaṃ carati rocamānam । tasminn annaṃ saha devatābhiḥ ।। cakṣuḥ śrotraṃ janayan brahma medhām ।
vācaṃ śreṣṭhāṃ yaśo asmāsu dhehy ।। annaṃ reto lohitam udaraṃ tāni kalpan । tapo atiṣṭhat tapyamānaḥ samudre ।। anuvāka ।।
brahma yajñaḥ pṛthivīṃ dhārayanti । asaṃbādhaṃ madhyato mānaveṣu ।। nānāvīryā oṣadhīr yā bibharti । pṛthivī naḥ prathatāṃ rādhyatāṃ naḥ ।।
yasyāṃ devā anṛtam anvavindan । sā no bhūmir goṣv aśveṣv apy anne kṛṇotu ।। yasyāṃ devā asurān abhyavartayan । sā no bhūmiḥ pūrvapeye dadhātu ।।
yasyām annaṃ kṛṣṭayaḥ saṃbabhūvuḥ । bhagaṃ varcaḥ pṛthivī no dadhātu ।। hiraṇyavakṣā jagato niveśanīḥ । indrarṣabhā draviṇe no dadhātu ।।
ahorātre apramādaṃ kṣaranti । atho ukṣatu varcasā ।। devā bhūmiṃ pṛthivīm apramādam । atho ukṣatu varcasā ।।
yāṃ māyābhir anvacaran manīṣiṇaḥ । satyenāvṛtam amṛtaṃ pṛthivyāḥ । sā no bhūmis tviṣiṃ balaṃ rāṣṭre dadhātu me ।। viṣṇur yasyāṃ vicakrame ।
anamitrāṃ chacīpatiḥ । mātā putrāya naḥ payaḥ ।। araṇyan te pṛthivi syonam astu naḥ । ajīto ahato akṣato adhyaṣṭhāṃ pṛthivīm aham ।।
yās ta ūrjas tanvaḥ saṃbabhūvuḥ । tāsu no dhehy abhi naḥ pavasva ।। parjanyaḥ pitā sa u naḥ pipartu ।। yasyāṃ yajñaṃ tanvate viśvakarmāṇaḥ ।
ūrdhvāḥ śukrā āhutyāḥ purastāt । sā no bhūmir vardhayād vardhamānā ।। yo abhimanyātai manasā vadhena । tan no bhūme randhaya pūrvakṛtvane ।।
tvaṃ bibharṣi dvipadaś catuṣpadaḥ । udyan sūryo raśmibhir ā tanoti ।। vāco madhu pṛthivī dhehi mahyam ।। dhruvāṃ bhūmiṃ pṛthivīṃ dharmaṇā dhṛtām ।
śivāṃ syonām anu carema viśvahā ।। mahān vega ejathur vepathuṣ ṭe । hiraṇyasyeva saṃdṛśi ।। agnim āpo bibhraty agnir aśmasu ।
goṣv aśveṣv agnayaḥ ।। agner devasyorv antarikṣam । havyavāhaṃ ghṛtapriyam ।। tviṣīmantaṃ saṃśitaṃ mā kṛṇotu ।
yajñaṃ havyam araṃkṛtam । svadhayānnena martyāḥ । jaradaṣṭiṃ mā pṛthivī kṛṇotu ।। yaṃ bibhraty oṣadhayo yam āpaḥ ।
yas te gām aśvam arhati । mā no dvikṣata kaś cana ।। yaṃ saṃjabhruḥ sūryāyā vivāhe । amartyāḥ pṛthivi gandham agre ।
mā no dvikṣata kaś cana ।। yo vadhūṣu vadhūyuṣu । yo mṛgeṣūta hastiṣu । mā no dvikṣata kaś cana ।।
yā bhūmiḥ saṃbhṛtā dhṛtā । dhruvās tiṣṭhanti viśvahā । dhṛtām acchā vadāmasi ।। tiṣṭhantaḥ prakrāmantaḥ ।
mā vyathiṣmahi bhūmyām ।। kṣamāṃ bhūmiṃ brahmaṇā vāvṛdhānām । ghṛtaṃ tvābhi ni ṣīdāmi bhūme ।। yo me sehur apriye taṃ ni dadhmaḥ ।
pavitreṇa pṛthivīm ut punāmi ।। maṇiṃ hiraṇyaṃ pṛthivī dadhātu naḥ । devī dadhātu sumanasyamānā ।। yās te bhūme adharād yāś ca paścāt ।
mā ni paptaṃ bhuvane śiśriyāṇe ।। mā vidan paripanthinaḥ ।। bhūme sūryeṇa medinā । -uttarām uttarāṃ samām ।।
oṣaṃ tad api rohatu । mā te hṛdayam arpipam ।। dakṣiṇaṃ savyam abhi bhūme pārśvam । sarvasya pratiśīvari ।।
śarad dhemantaḥ śiśiro vasantaḥ । ahorātre pṛthivī no duhātām ।। yasyām āsann agnayo apsv antaḥ । śakrāya dadhre vṛṣabhāya vṛṣṇe ।
sa no bhūmer ā diśatu yad dhanaṃ kāmayāmahe ।। indro yātu purogavaḥ । yūpo yasyāṃ nimīyate । ṛgbhiḥ sāmnā yajurvidaḥ ।
somam indrāya pātave । suśevā yajñe dadhātu sumanasyamānā ।। ṛṣayo gā udānṛcuḥ । yajñena tapasā saha ।
dīrghaṃ ma āyuḥ savitā kṛṇotu ।। yatremāḥ pañca kṛṣṭayaḥ । namo astu varṣam edhate ।। janā martyā vailavāḥ ।
yasyāṃ vadati dundubhiḥ । yo no dveṣṭy adharaṃ taṃ kṛṇotu ।। kṣetre yasyāṃ vikurvate । āśāmāśāṃ raṇyāṃ naḥ kṛṇotu ।।
nānādharmāṇaṃ pṛthivī yathaukasam । dhruveva dhenur anapasphurantī ।। hemantajabdho bhṛmalo guhā śaye । yac chivaṃ tena no mṛḍa ।।
rathasya vartman manasaś ca yātave । taṃ panthāṃ jayemānamitram ataskaram ।। bhadrapāpasya nidhanaṃ titikṣuḥ । varāhāya vi jihīte mṛgāya ।।
siṃhā vyāghrāḥ puruṣādaś caranti । ṛkṣīkāṃ rakṣo apa badhāsmat ।। ye carāyāḥ kimīdinaḥ । tān asmad bhūme yāvaya ।।
haṃsāḥ suparṇāḥ śakunā vayāṃsi । rajāṃsi kṛṇvaṃś cyāvayaṃś ca vṛkṣān । ahorātre vihite bhūmyām adhi ।। varṣeṇa bhūmiḥ pṛthivī vṛtāvṛtā ।
priye dhāmanidhāmani ।। -antarikṣaṃ ca me vyacaḥ । viśve devāś ca saṃ dadhuḥ ।। uttaro nāma bhūmyām ।
āśāmāśāṃ viṣāsahiḥ ।। devaiḥ sṛṣṭā vyasarpo mahitvam । akalpayathāḥ pradiśaś catasraḥ ।। yāḥ sabhā adhi bhūmyām ।
udyāsaṃ madhumad vacaḥ ।। yad īkṣe ṣutadyaḥ punantu mā । tviṣīmān asmi jūtimān yān hanmi dodhataḥ ।। ya ākṣiyan pṛthivīm ād ajāyata ।
vanaspatīnāṃ gṛbhir oṣadhīnām ।। kīlālodhnī payasvatī । pṛthivī payasā saha ।। bhadrayā supratiṣṭhitam ।
śriyāṃ mā dhehi bhūtyām ।। yasyām āsann agnayo apsv antaḥ । -āsīd āvir bhogair abhavan mātṛmadbhiḥ ।। aditiḥ kāmadughā viśvarūpā ।
prajāpatiḥ prajābhiḥ saṃvidānaḥ ।। anuvāka ।। kasminn aṅga ṛtam asyādhyāhitam । kasminn aṅge satyam asya pratiṣṭhitam ।।
kasminn aṅge diśo asya pratiṣṭhitāḥ । ahorātre saṃvidāne samānam ।। kasminn aṅge tiṣṭhaty antarikṣam । kasminn aṅge tiṣṭhaty uttaraṃ divaḥ ।।
kasmād aṅgāt pavate mātariśvā । skambhasya mahad vimimāno aṅgam ।। kva prepsan pavate mātariśvā । skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ ।।
ahorātre dravataḥ saṃvidāne । skambhaṃ ।। saṃvatsareṇa saha saṃvidānāḥ । skambhaṃ ।।
lokān sarvām̐ adhārayat । skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ ।। prajāpatiḥ sasṛje viśvarūpam । yan na pārviśat kva tad babhūva ।।
kiyad bhaviṣyad anvāśaye asya । kiyatā skambhaḥ pra viveśa tatra ।। brahma yatra janā viduḥ । skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ ।।
ṛtaṃ dhārayaty uttaram । skambhaṃ ।। dyaur asminn adhyāhitā । skambhaṃ ।।
aṅge sarve samāhitāḥ । skambhaṃ ।। ṛcaḥ sāma yajur mahī । skambhaṃ ।।
nāḍyas tiṣṭhanti prapyasāḥ । skambhaṃ ।। puruṣaś ca samāhitāḥ । skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ ।।
te skambham anu saṃ viduḥ । yaś ca veda prajāpatim । te skambham anu saṃ viduḥ ।। cakṣur aṅgiraso abhavan ।
skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ ।। jihvāṃ madhukaśām uta । skambhaṃ ।। yajur yasmād apākaṣan ।
skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ ।। paramam iva janā viduḥ । vasavaś ca samāhitāḥ । skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ ।।
nidhiṃ rakṣanti sarvadā । yaṃ devā abhirakṣata ।। brahma jyeṣṭham upāsate । taṃ vai brahmavido viduḥ ।।
asatas pari jajñire । -asad āhuḥ paro janāḥ ।। purāṇaṃ vyavartayat । purāṇam anu saṃ viduḥ ।।
aṅgā gātrāṇi bhejire । eke brahmavido viduḥ ।। anatyudyaṃ janā viduḥ । dhiraṇyaṃ loke antarā ।।
skambhe adhy ṛtam āhitam । indre sarvaṃ samāhitam ।। indre adhy ṛtam āhitam । skambhe sarvaṃ samāhitam ।।
purā sūryāt puroṣasaḥ । yasmān na param asti bhūtam ।। yasya bhūmiḥ pramāntarikṣam utodaram । tasmai jyeṣṭhāya brahmaṇe namaḥ ।।
candramāś ca punar navaḥ । tasmai jyeṣṭhāya brahmaṇe namaḥ ।। cakṣur aṅgiraso abhuvan । tasmai jyeṣṭhāya brahmaṇe namaḥ ।।
lokān sarvān samānaśe । tasmai jyeṣṭhāya brahmaṇe namaḥ ।। skambho dādhārorv antarikṣam । skambha idaṃ viśvaṃ bhuvanam ā viveśa ।।
kathaṃ na ramate manaḥ । pra caṅkramīti sarvadā ।। tapasi krāntaṃ salilasya pṛṣṭhe । vṛkṣasya skambhaṃ parita iva śākhāḥ ।।
vācā śrotreṇa cakṣuṣā । skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ ।। vyāvṛttaḥ sa pāpmanā । yāni trīṇi prajāpatau ।।
tiṣṭhantaṃ salile veda । sa vai guhyaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।। nāty eti parameṣṭhinam । yaj jyeṣṭhaṃ paro atyayat ।।
asti vai tat paro divaḥ । yasminn otāḥ prajā imāḥ ।। anuvāka ।। dūrśe durnihitaiṣiṇi ।
nāmadheyāni vidmasi । naśyatetaḥ sadānvāḥ ।। urukīṃ keśinīṃ krakum । nāśayāmaḥ sadānvāḥ ।।
asaṃsūktanigāriṇīm । naśyatetaḥ sadānvāḥ ।। naktam icchanty āturam । tā ito nāśayāmasi ।।
vastagandhāḥ sadānvāḥ । tīkṣṇaśṛṅga ivarṣabhaḥ ।। strīpuṃsām̐ ubhayān saha । vi mṛdho hanmi rakṣasaḥ ।।
dīrghakeśām̐ asṛnmukhān । durṇāmno nāśayāmasi ।। rodākām̐ rudatīṃ tvat । nāśayāmaḥ sadānvāḥ ।।
upa vṛkṣeṣu śerate । ।। śālā icchanti satvaram । nāśayāmaḥ sadānvāḥ ।।
kṣetrād uptād varpitāta । naśyatetaḥ sadānvāḥ ।। sadā rukṣā visṛkpadī । nirajetaḥ śacīpate ।।
na va ihāsti nyañcanam । garbhān āṇḍāni bhetsyati ।। mṛṇīhi durṇaśīṃ kuham । nāśayāmaḥ sadānvāḥ ।।
ajamāyuṃ ca nighnatīm । nāśayāmaḥ sadānvāḥ ।। yūyaṃ bhaṇvāḥ sadānvāḥ । -āt surām ava mehatha ।।
atho śīrṣakty ā śaye । nāśayāmaḥ sadānvāḥ ।। vṛkṣāṇāṃ yantu satvaram । pra mṛśantv arāyyaḥ ।।
hasanaikā kanikradā । nāmadheyāni vidmasi । naśyatetaḥ sadānvāḥ ।। imāṃ śālāṃ viṣāsahim ।
jaitrāyācchā vadāmasi ।। arāyi kim ihecchase । ni stauṣāmi sadānve ।। kim ic chāntyabhiśrayā ।
tā ito nāśayāmasi ।। ānṛtyantīṃ kutūhalām । tā ito nāśayāmasi ।। -urarā ghoracakṣavaḥ ।
paro bhrūṇāny arpaya ।। paryaiti puruṣaṃ pathi । jātavedāḥ sadānvāḥ ।। śūnyam agnau jighatsanti ।
tā ito nāśayāmasi ।। vaḍavā gardabhīr iva । nāśayāmaḥ sadānvāḥ ।। yā adanti sadānvāḥ ।
tā ito nāśayāmasi ।। -indrajā naḥ sadānvāḥ । punas tā prati dadmasi ।। anagnigandhyādinīḥ ।
śavam atta sadānvāḥ । kim u śālāsv icchatha ।। yuvatīr yāḥ sadānvāḥ । arāyīr abhibhā itaḥ ।।
tviṣim adhvagaghātinīm । vajreṇānaparādhinā । indra bhaṇvāḥ phalīkuru ।। yā adanti prakhādinīḥ ।
yā devo viśvād rakṣāṃsi sedhati ।। manuṣyebhyaś ca yāḥ kṛtāḥ । parāvataṃ navatiṃ nāvyā ati ।। vṛkāṇām iva gaṅgaṇaḥ ।
nāśayāmaḥ sadānvāḥ ।। rātrīṃ yakṣāṇi prerate । viśvād rakṣāṃsi sedhatu ।। -apsu jātāḥ pulīkayāḥ ।
tā ito nāśayāmasi ।। śiśumākāṃ pratiśrukām । atiduhnāṃ vicalantīṃ vitūlumām । nāśayāmaḥ sadānvāḥ ।।
taṃstanīkāṃ vṛṅktapadīm । nāśayāmaḥ sadānvāḥ ।। vijavrāṃ labruvaṃ lavum । nāśayāmaḥ sadānvāḥ ।।
anuvāka ।। anu cainām abhutsata । tat prajāvad apatyavat ।। paśubhiś copa dasyati ।
devānāṃ gāṃ na ditsati ।। śroṇayā kāṭam ardati । kāṇayā jīyate svam ।। chakno vindati gopatim ।
duradabhnā hy ucyase ।। ā sa deveṣu vṛścate । kanīyaḥ kṛṇute svam ।। viklindur nāma vindati ।
yā mukhenopajighrati ।। loma dhvāṅkṣo ajīhiḍat । vatsāṃś ca ghātuko vṛkaḥ ।। bālān kaś cit pra kṛntati ।
yakṣmaś chantsaty anāmanāt ।। śakṛd dāsī samasyati । tasmād avyeṣyad enasaḥ ।। devān sabrāhmaṇān vaśā ।
tad āhuḥ svasya gopanam ।। teṣāṃ devakṛtā vaśā । ya enāṃ nipriyāyate ।। ārṣeyebhyo na ditsati ।
brāhmanānāṃ ca manyave ।। anyām iccheta tarhi saḥ । yācitāṃ ca na ditsati ।। brāhmaṇānāṃ tathā vaśā ।
yasmin kasmiṃś ca jāyate ।। yad vaśāṃ brāhmaṇā abhi । evāsyānirodhanam ।। avijñātagadā satī ।
brāhmaṇas tarhy eṣyaḥ ।। devānāṃ nihitaṃ nidhim । parikramyeṣum asyataḥ ।। yācitāṃ ca na ditsati ।
yam adattvā cikīrṣati ।। -atho asyā stanān uta । dātuṃ ced aśakad vaśām ।। mukhaṃ kṛtvā brahmaṇam ।
dheḍaṃ ny eti mānuṣaḥ ।। brāhmaṇebhyo adadad vaśām । martyaś cen nipriyāyate ।। brāhmaṇā gopatiṃ vaśām ।
evaṃ ha viduṣo vaśā ।। -anyasmai dadad vaśām । pṛthivī sahadevatā ।। yasminn agre ajāyata ।
saha devair ud ājata ।। vaśā kṛṇotu pūruṣam । athaināṃ ni priyāyate ।। mitrāya varuṇāya ca ।
tebhya ā vṛścate adadhat ।। -upaśṛṇuyād ṛcaḥ svayam । nāsya śrutā gṛhe syāt ।। -atha goṣv acīcarat ।
devā vṛścanti hīḍitāḥ ।। devānāṃ nihito nidhiḥ । yathā sthāma jigāṃsati ।। yathā sthāma jigāṃsati ।
yākyāya kṛṇute manaḥ ।। tad devām̐ api gacchati । upaprayanti yācitum ।। yajñena devatābhyaḥ ।
mātur heḍaṃ na gacchati ।। tathā saṃbhūtam agraśaḥ । ya brahmabhyaḥ pradīyate ।। ālumpet sruco agnaye ।
āgnaye vṛścate adadhat ।। loke asyopa tiṣṭhati । vaśā pradaduṣe bahūn ।। vaśā pradaduṣe duhe ।
nirundhānasya yācitām ।। kruddhā gopataye vaśā । mṛtyoḥ pāśeṣu badhyatām ।। gṛheṣu pacate vaśām ।
yācayate bṛhaspatiḥ ।। carantī goṣu gaur api । daduṣe viṣaṃ duhe ।। yad brahmabhyaḥ pradīyate ।
yad devatrā haviḥ syāt ।। devā yajñād udetya । udākuruta nāradaḥ ।। vaśeyāṃ na vaśeti ।
eṣā vaśānāṃ vaśatamā ।। yās tvaṃ vettha manuṣyajāḥ । kasyā nāśnīyād abrāhmaṇaḥ ।। yā ca sūtavaśā vaśā ।
ya āśaṃseti bhūtyām ।। -anuṣṭha viduṣe vaśā । yām adattvā parābhavet ।। yā ca sūtavaśā vaśā ।
ya āśaṃśeti bhūtyām ।। viliptī sūtavaśā vaśā । syonāvaskaḥ prajāpatau ।। iti manvīta yācitaḥ ।
yā bhīmādaduṣo gṛhe ।। na no dād iti hīḍitāḥ । tasmād vai sa parābhavat ।। vaśām indreṇa yācitaḥ ।
vṛścann ahamuttare ।। vadanti parirāpinaḥ । ā vṛścante acityā ।। -athāhur mā dadā iti ।
pari yanty acetasaḥ ।। amā ca pacate vaśām । jihmo lokān nir ṛcchati ।। anuvāka ।।
asṛṅ māṃsaṃ tvacaṃ peṣṭraṃ mastṛhaṇaṃ majjñaḥ śarīram । agniḥ kravyād attv amuṣyāmuṣyāyaṇasyāmuṣyāḥ putrasya ।। prātaryāvadbhyo devebhyaḥ sāyaṃyāvadbhyo devebhyo viśvadānīṃyāvadbhyo devebhyaḥ । amuṣyāmuṣyāyaṇam amuṣyāḥ putram ā vṛścāmi ।।
vaiśvānarāya kṣipradhanvane amum āmuṣyāyaṇam amuṣyāḥ putram ā vṛścāmi ।। kṣipradhanvan kṣiprahasta । amuṣyāmuṣyāyaṇasyāmuṣyāḥ putrasya hṛdayaṃ yakṛn matasne pra vidhya ।। indrāgnibhyāṃ prajāpataye parameṣṭhine somāya rājñe varuṇāya rājñe ।
pūṣṇe dhātre savitre tvaṣṭre amum āmuṣyāyaṇam amuṣyāḥ putram ā vṛścāmi ।। uṣase ahne rātraye sūryāyāmum ।। vīrudbhya oṣadhībhyo vanaspatibhyo vānaspatebhyo amum ।। adbhyo mātariśvane adyāvāpṛthivībhyām amum ।।
idāvatsarāya parivatsarāya saṃvatsarāya bṛhate viśvarūpāyāmum ।। mādbhyaḥ saṃvatsarāyāmum ।। digbhyo antardeśebhya āśābhya āśāpālebhyo amum ।। ṛtubhya ārtavebhyo adhipatibhya ādhipatyebhyo amum ।। ṛṣibhya ārṣeyebhyo aṅgirobhya āṅgirasebhyo atharvabhya ātharvaṇebhyo amum ।। vasubhyo rudrebhya ādityebhyaḥ sādhyebhya āptyebhyo amum ।। amum āmuṣyāyaṇam amuṣyāḥ putram ā vṛścāmi ।।
ye svaś cakrur ye svar jajñuḥ । tebhyaḥ svaḥkṛdbhyaḥ svaḥkārebhyo amum āmuṣyāyaṇam amuṣyāḥ putram ā vṛścāmi । te svaḥkṛtaḥ svaḥkārā amum āmuṣyāyaṇam amuṣyāḥ putraṃ parā bhāvayantu ।। ye tapaś cakrur ye tapo jajñuḥ ।
tebhyas tapaskṛdbhyas tapaskārebhyo amum । te tapaskṛtas tapaskārā amum ।। ye brahma cakrur ye brahma jajñuḥ । tebhyo brahmakṛdbhyo brahmakārebhyo amum āmuṣyāyaṇam amuṣyāḥ putram ā vṛścāmi ।
te brahmakṛto brahmakārā amum āmuṣyāyaṇam amuṣyāḥ putraṃ parā bhāvayantu ।। aghāriṇīm amūm aghaviddhāṃ vikeśīm apapratidhimāsoktīṃ devamanuṣyāḥ paśyantu । amum āmuṣyāyaṇam amuṣyāḥ putraṃ rurudhuṣīm ।। aliklavā gṛdhrāḥ kaṅkāḥ suparṇāḥ śvapadāḥ patatriṇaḥ ।
vayāṃsi śakunayo amuṣyāmuṣyāyaṇasyāmuṣyāḥ putrasyādahane carantu ।। -avadyaṃ ca malaṃ ca yat । yad ṛcānṛtam ūdima ।। tā no muñcaṃtv aṃhasaḥ ।।
atho varuṇyād uta । viśvasmād devaduṣkṛtāt ।। druho mā muñcantu varuṇasya pāśāt ।। mahyam indro varuṇo bṛhaspatiḥ savitā varca ādadhan ।।
bhrātṛvyahaṃ sapatnaham asau me bhrātṛbhyo asau sapatnaḥ ।। tam adharāñcaṃ mṛtyupatham abhyapa nudāmi ।। pāpmanaḥ putro asy abhūtyā adhi jāto yamasya karaṇaḥ । taṃ tvā svapna tathā vidma ।
yaḥ pāpas taṃ dviṣate pra hiṇmaḥ । vaiśvāṇarasyainaṃ daṃṣṭrayor api dadhmaḥ ।। grāhyāḥ putro asi nirṛtyā adhi ।। varuṇasya putro asi varuṇānyā adhi ।।
ahnaḥ putro asi rātryā adhi ।। divas putro asi bhūmyā adhi ।। vanaspatīnāṃ putro asy oṣadībhyo adhi ।। vānaspatyānāṃ putro asi vīrudbhyo adhi ।।
tandriyāḥ putro asi koṭīyā adhi ।। rakṣasāṃ putro asy abhvebhyo adhi ।। apsarobhyo adhi jāto yamasya karaṇaḥ । taṃ tvā svapna iti trīṇi ।।
dyāvāpṛthivī ahorātre nakṣatrapeśaḥ । idam aham amuṣminn āmuṣyāyaṇe amuṣyāḥ putre duṣvapnyaṃ vrajet ।। yad asmāsv ity āṣṭādaśakī ।। mā yajñād indra sominaḥ ।
mānta sthur no arātayaḥ ।। tantur deveṣv ātataḥ । tam āhutam aśīmahi ।। maho devāya tad ṛtaṃ saparyata ।
divas putrāya sūryāya śaṃsata ।। na te adevaḥ pradivo vi vāsati । ud anyena jyotiṣā yāsi sūrya ।। jagac ca viśvam abhīyarṣi bhānunā ।
apāmīvām apa duṣvapnyaṃ suva ।। amuṣmā āmuṣyāyaṇāyāmuṣyāḥ putrāya pra hiṇmaḥ ।। dyāvāpṛthivī vahataṃ duṣvapnyaṃ parā vahataṃ duṣvapnyam । amuṣmā āmuṣyāyaṇāyāmuṣyāḥ putrāya ।।
vātāpavamānau vahatam ।। indrāgnī vahatam ।। mitrāvaruṇā vahatam ।। bhavāśarvau vahatam ।।
devāśvinā vahataṃ duṣvapnyaṃ parā vahataṃ duṣvapnyam । ।। devā maruto vahata duṣvapnyaṃ parā vahata duṣvapnyam । ।।
devāḥ pitaro vahata duṣvapnyaṃ parā vahata duṣvapnyam । ।। deva sūrya vaha duṣvapnyaṃ parā vaha duṣvapnyam । ।।
deva candramo vaha duṣvapnyaṃ parā vaha duṣvapnyam । ।। devā nakṣatrāṇi vahata duṣvapnyaṃ parā vahata duṣvapnyam । ।।
devīr āpo vahata duṣvapnyaṃ parā vahata duṣvapnyam । ।। deva viṣṇo vaha duṣvapnyam ।। deva tvaṣṭar vaha ।।
deva dhātar vaha ।। deva savitar vaha ।। deva pūṣan vaha ।। deva bṛhaspate vaha ।।
deva prajāpate vaha ।। deva parameṣṭhin vaha duṣvapnyaṃ parā vaha duṣvapnyam । ।। ahorātre vahataṃ duṣvapnyaṃ parā vahataṃ duṣvapnyam ।
amuṣmā āmuṣyāyaṇāyāmuṣyāḥ putrāya ।। anuvāka ।। indro vajram asiñcad vṛtrāya hantave । tvaṣṭā vajram asiñcad vṛtrāya hantave ।।
yad dhārambhaṇaṃ sa vaiśvānaraḥ ।। etad vā idaṃ sarvaṃ yad etāni trīṇi । viśvānaro vaiśvānaro viśvāṣāṭ ।। ya evaṃ vidvān anaḍuho vrataṃ bibharti ।।
tam upāmimīta pra harāṇīti ।। daivo vajraḥ kṣuraḥ paviḥ sahasrapṛṣṭir divispṛśaḥ ।। sa saṃśiñjāno atiṣṭhad dhariharā bhavann etad ṛcchan ।। sa samudram adahat ।।
vaiśvānareṇa hi dagdhaḥ ।। vrataṃ carāṇīti sa vratam acarat ।। aṇur hi kṛśo bhūtvendro asurān apāvṛṅkta ।। sa parameṣṭhinam upādhāvat ।।
sa prajāpatim upādhāvat ।। sa viṣṇum upādhāvat ।। sa gṛhapatim upādhāvat ।। sa virājam upādhāvat ।।
sa svarājam upādhāvat ।। sa samrājam upādhāvat ।। so ahorātre upadhāvat ।। so ardhamāsān upādhāvat ।।
sa māsān upādhāvat ।। sa ṛtūn upādhāvat ।। sa ārtavān upādhāvat ।। sa ṛṣīn upādhāvat ।।
sa ārṣeyān upādhāvat ।। so aṅgirasa upapādhāvat ।। sa āṅgirasān upādhāvat ।। so atharvaṇa upādhāvat ।।
sa ātharvaṇān upādhāvat ।। somaḥ prathamo athendrāgnī ।। so aśāmyat ।। tasmād yo brahma vedotāpaskṛtaṃ śamayati dohayata evainān ।।
tam ṛksāmābhyām ādatta yajuṣā yajñena gāyatreṇa vāmadevyena ca ।। etad vā idaṃ sarvaṃ yad ṛksāme etāv indrasya bāhū ।। tam ādatta taṃ paruṣy ādhatta ।। prajā vai samṛddhir akṣitiḥ paśavaḥ parūṃṣi ।।
yaḥ ।। [see sa dikṣu praty atiṣṭhat ।। yaḥ ।। sa viśvāṣāhy akramat ।।eṣā vai viṣvāṣāḍ ḍyaur evāsau ।। ete vai sarve puṇyā lokāḥ sarvāś ca devatāḥ sa nādhārayat ।।
yaḥ ।। sa viśvānare akramata ।।eṣa vai viśvānaro yad antarikṣaṃ samudraḥ ।।ete vai pathayo devayānā yat sūryasya raśmayaḥ saḥ ।। yaḥ ।। sa vaiśvānare akramata ।।eṣa vai vaiśvānaro yad ayaṃ pavamānaḥ ।।eṣa vai sarvā anuprajāto dhriyate sa nādhārayat ।।
yaḥ ।। sa vṛtre akramata ।। tasya vṛtrasyāṅgā parvāṇi śarīrāṇy abhajyanta । etāni vai vṛtrasyāṅgā parvāṇi śarīrāṇi yad ime parvatāḥ ।।
sa yatra hṛdā manasā kāmayata iha me rādhyate tad asmai rādhyate ।। yaḥ ।। āśaṃsāmahe gurv etad vratam āraṇyeṣu paśuṣu grāmyeṣv aty eti ।। varaṃ vṛṇīṣveti sa varam avṛṇīta ।।
bradhnaloko asāni bradhnasya viṣṭapi śrayā iti ।। ṣoḍaśo vā ita ūrdhvo loko yad bradhno yad bradhnasya viṣṭapaḥ ।। yaḥ ।। ned iṣṭāpūrtena vi bhavānīti ।।
yad anaḍvān yad anaḍudvratī ।। -iṣṭam evāsya pūrtaṃ māyāṃ saṃ vṛkte ।। teṣām iṣṭaṃ pūrtaṃ māyāṃ saṃvṛktānindraṃ hy enam ।। sarvām̐l lokān prājānāt ।।
yāv aparapādau tāv aparapakṣau ।। ye nāsike tau sruvau ।। yāni vakṣaṇāni te sūryasya raśmayaḥ saḥ ।। droṇakalaśaḥ śiraḥ somo rājā mastiṣkaḥ ।।
ye asya śṛṅge tad ṛtaṃ satyam ।। dhruvaṃ vā ṛtaṃ satyaṃ tasmād ete dhruve ।। yaḥ ।। yāv asya karṇau sā śraddhā ।।
tasmāt karṇau muhur varīvarjayati ।। yaḥ ।। yāsya dakṣiṇā hanuḥ sā juhur yā savyā sopabhṛd yaḥ kaṇṭhaḥ sā dhruvā ।।agnir āsyaṃ vidyuj jihvā maruto dantāḥ pavamānaḥ prāṇaḥ ।।eṣā vai sā yām āhur vasor dhāreti yad āntragudam ।। yaḥ ।।
yad asya carmaṃ tad abhraṃ yāni lomāni tāni nakṣatrāṇi ।।svedo varṣam ūṣmā nīhāra oṣadhayaś ca vanaspatayaś cobadhyam ।।yo asya dakṣiṇo ardhas tau śāradau māsau yaḥ savyas tau haimanau ।।yo asya jaghanārdhas tau śaiśirau māsau yaḥ pūrvādhas tau vāsantau ।।yad asya pṛṣṭhaṃ tau graiṣmau māsau yan madhyau tau vārṣikau ।।saṃvatsaro vā eṣa saṃbhṛto yad anaḍvān yad anaḍudvratī ।। yaḥ ।। yad asminn antar ṛcaḥ sāmāni yajūṃṣi brāhmaṇam ।। yaḥ ।।
atha yad asminn antaḥ ।।śataṃ śraddhā śataṃ dīkṣāḥ śataṃ yajñāḥ śataṃ dakṣiṇāḥ ।।śataṃ bhūtayaḥ śataṃ puṣṭayaḥ śataṃ prabhūtayaḥ śataṃ samṛddhayaḥ ।।śatam abhūtayaḥ śataṃ nirbhūtayaḥ śataṃ parābhūtayaḥ śatam asamṛddhayaḥ ।।śatamadhyāni śatam algaṇāni śataṃ tamāṃsi śataṃ rudhirāṇi ।।ya evaṃ viduṣo asādhu kīrtayaty etair evainaṃ tamobhiḥ prorṇoti ।।yad asya prācīnaṃ nābhyās tena dviṣantam ā viśati ।।atha yad asya pratīcīnaṃ nābhyās tena mṛtuṃ nāṣṭrām avartiṃ tarati ।। yaḥ ।। śatam ardhamāsāḥ śataṃ māsāḥ śatam ṛtavaḥ śatam ārtavāḥ ।।śatam idāvatsarāḥ śataṃ parivatsarāḥ śataṃ saṃvatsarāḥ ।।śataṃ brahmāṇi śataṃ karmāṇi śataṃ jyotīṃṣi śatam amṛtāni ।।śataṃ prāṇāḥ śatam apānāḥ śataṃ vyānāḥ śataṃ samānāḥ ।। yaḥ ।।
atha yad asminn antaḥ ।।śataṃ gāyatrāḥ śataṃ sāhnāḥ śataṃ trirātrāḥ śatam atirātrāḥ ।।śatam agniṣṭomāḥ śataṃ dvādaśāhāḥ śataṃ ṣoḍaśinaḥ śataṃ sarvapṛṣṭhyāḥ ।।śataṃ rājāsūyāḥ śataṃ vājapeyāḥ śataṃ kāmaprāḥ sahasraṃ satrāyaṇāni ।।eṣa vānaḍvān sarvāṅgaḥ sarvātmā sarvaparuḥ sarvapān madhyataḥ praty aṣṭhāt ।।ṛksāmābhyām uttabhito yajuṣā yajñena gāyatreṇa brahmaṇā prathita upariṣṭāt ।। yaḥ ।। indro balenāsi parameṣṭhī vratena gaus tena vaiśvadevaḥ ।। tasya prāṇān saṃ vṛha tasya prāṇān vi vṛha ।।
indro asīndrasya rūpam asi prajāpatir asi parameṣṭhy asi ।। svar asi svargo asi svargaloko asi svargaṃ mā lokaṃ gamaya ।। yenāsya vahas tena yajño yena vahati tena lokaḥ ।। yenainaṃ paśyati tena viśvo yenainaṃ gamayati tena sarvaḥ ।।
ye asya pādāḥ sā pratiṣṭhā । ya evaṃ vidvān anaḍuho vrataṃ bibharti ।। anuvāka ।। idaṃ sīsaṃ bhāgadheyaṃ ta ehi ।
tena tvaṃ sākam adharāṅ parehi ।। kareṇānukareṇa ca । yakṣmāṃś ca nir ajāmasi ।। nir yakṣmam ajāmasi ।
yaṃ dviṣmas taṃ te pra suvāmaḥ ।। imaṃ goṣṭham anyokā ā viveśa । dūraṃ sa gacchatv apsuṣado aty agnīn ।। manyunā puruṣe mṛte ।
punas tvod dīpayāmasi ।। punar brahmā vasunītir agre । dīrghāyutvāya śataśāradāya ।। imaṃ paśyann itaraṃ jātavedasam ।
sa gharmam indhat parame sadhasthe ।। yamarājño gacchatu ripravāhaḥ । devo devebhyo havyaṃ vahatu prajānan ।। janān druhantaṃ vajreṇa mṛtyum ।
pitṝṇāṃ loke api bhāgo asya ।। pra hiṇomi pathibhiḥ pitṛyāṇaiḥ । atraivaidhi pitṛṣu jāgṛhi tvam ।। śuddhā bhavantaḥ śucayaḥ pāvakāḥ ।
samiddho agniḥ supunā punāti ।। divas pṛṣṭhāny āruhat । mohyāsmām̐ aśastyāḥ ।। agne riprāṇi mṛjmahe ।
pra ṇa āyūṃṣi tāriṣat ।। nirṛtho yaś ca nisvaraḥ । dūrād dūram acucyavuḥ ।। gobhyo aśvebhyas tvā ।
agniṃ jīvitayopanam ।। yo goṣu yo ajādiṣu । agnir yo janayopanaḥ ।। sa no mābhyapakramīḥ ।
jyok ca sūryāya dṛśe ।। yasmin manuṣyā uta । tvam agne divaṃ ruha ।। agniḥ saṃkasukaś ca yaḥ ।
śīrṣaktim upabarhaṇe ।। śīrṣaktim upabarhaṇe । śuddhā bhavanti yajñiyāḥ ।। yas ta eṣa itaro devayānāt ।
-iha me vīrā bahavo bhavantu ।। abhūd bhadrā devahūtir no adya । suvīrāso vidatham ā vadema ।। maiṣāṃ nu gād aparo artham etam ।
tiro mṛtyuṃ dadhatāṃ parvatena ।। yathartava ṛtubhir yanti sākam । evā tvaṣṭar āyuṃṣi kalpayaiṣām ।। anupūrvaṃ yatamānā yati ṣṭha ।
sarvam āyur nayatu jīvanāya ।। vīrayadhvaṃ pra taratā sakhāyaḥ । anamīvān ut taremābhi vājān ।। 'śmanvatī syandate nadīyam ।
śivān syonān ut taremābhi vājān ।। śuddhā bhavantaḥ śucayaḥ pāvakāḥ । śataṃ himāḥ sarvavīrā madema ।। atikrāmanto avarān parebhiḥ ।
mṛtyuṃ pratyauhan padayopanena ।। drāghīya āyuḥ prataraṃ dadhānāḥ । atha jīvā vidatham ā vadema ।। āñjanena sarpiṣā saṃ viśantu ।
ā rohantu janayo yonim agre ।। āñjanena sarpiṣā saṃ spṛśantām । syonād yoner adhi talpaṃ ruheyuḥ ।। tau brahmaṇā vy ahaṃ kalpayāmi ।
dīrghenāyuṣā sam imāṃ sṛjāmi ।। āviveśāmṛto martyeṣu । mā so asmān dvikṣata mā vayaṃ tam ।। kravyādā preta dakṣiṇā ।
brahmaṇe kṛṇuta priyam ।। pra kṣināty avartyā । yaḥ kravyād anirāhitaḥ ।। yac ca vastena vindate ।
kravyāc ced anirāhitaḥ ।। nainena havir attave । yaḥ kravyād anuvartate ।। ārtiṃ martyo ny eti ca ।
anuvidvān vitāvati ।। yat striyā mriyate patiḥ । yaḥ kravyādaṃ nir ādadhat ।। cakṛmā yac ca duṣkṛtam ।
agniḥ saṃkasukaś ca yaḥ ।। prajānatīḥ pathibhir devayānaiḥ । navāś caranti saritaḥ purāṇīḥ ।। agne akravyān niṣkravyādaṃ nudā devajanaṃ vaha ।।
-ayaṃ kravyādam anv agāt । taṃ harāmi śivāparam ।। ubhayān antarā śritaḥ । pitṝṇāṃ lokam upa yantu ye mṛtāḥ ।।
uṣāmuṣāṃ śreyasīṃśreyasīṃ dadhat । aiṣām ūrjaṃ rayim asmāsu dhehi ।। sa vo nividvān vijahātu mṛtyum । tena rudrasya pari pātāstām ।।
kṣemyas tiṣṭhan prataraṇaḥ suvīraḥ । jyog eva naḥ puruṣagandhir edhi ।। pāpaṃ jīvanti sarvadā । anuvidvān vitāvati ।।
muhur ā vartate punaḥ । aśva ivānuvapate naḍam ।। kravyādā samāsate । pary ādadhati sarvadā ।।
tilpiyaṃ daṇḍanaṃ naḍam । yamasyāgniṃ nirādadhau ।। sīsaṃ kravyād uta candraṃ ta āhuḥ । araṇyānyā gahvaraṃ sacasva ।।
pravidvān panthāṃ vi hy ācakāra । dīrgheṇāyuṣā sam adhād ihemān ।। sa vo nirvakṣad duritād avadyāt । ṣaḍbhir ūrmibhir amatiṃ carema ।।
yavena kṣudhaṃ puruhūta viśvām । ariṣṭāsa ṛjanībhis tarema ।। apāṃ rasair oṣadhīnāṃ ghṛtasya । sthirā vīrāḥ saṃmanaso bhavantu ।।
anuvāka ।। tatra hvayasva yatamā priyā te । tad vāṃ vayo yamarājye samānam ।। tāvac cakṣus tatidhā vājināni ।
adhā pakvān mithunā saṃ bhavāthaḥ ।। saṃ smā sametaṃ yamarājye । yadyad reto adhi vāṃ saṃbabhūva ।। imaṃ jīvaṃ jīvadhanyāḥ sam eta ।
yam odanaṃ pacati vo janitrī ।। riprān nirmukthyai śamalāc ca vācaḥ । ubhe vyāpa nabhasī mahitvā ।। ye yajvanām abhijitāḥ svargāḥ ।
tasmin putrair jarasi saṃ śrayethām ।। etaṃ lokaṃ śraddadhānāḥ sacante । sa vāṃ pakvaḥ pitryāṇe nyāyat ।। pary āvartethām abhi pātram etat ।
pakvāya śarma bahulaṃ ni yacchāt ।। yasyāṃ somo adhipā mṛḍitā ca । adhā pakvena saha saṃ bhavema ।। diśām udīcī kṛṇavan no agram ।
viśvair viśvāṅgaiḥ saha saṃ bhavema ।। śivā putrebhya uta mahyam astu । irya iva gopā abhi rakṣa pakvam ।। śivā no vātā iha vāntu śagmāḥ ।
taṃ nas tapa uta satyaṃ ma vittām ।। tsaraṃ viṣaktaṃ bila āsasāda । ulūkhalaṃ musalaṃ śundhatāpaḥ ।। pūtaḥ pavitrair apa hantu rakṣaḥ ।
mā dampatī pautram aghaṃ ni gātām ।। rakṣaḥ piśācām̐ apabādhamānaḥ । tena lokām̐ abhi sarvāñ jayema ।। ya eṣāṃ medasvān uta yaś cakarśa ।
sa naḥ svargam abhi neṣi lokam ।। saṃ jāyā saha putraiḥ syāma । mā nas tārīn nirṛtir mo arātiḥ ।। tamo vyasya pra vadāsi valgu ।
mā taṇḍulaṃ vi śarīr devayantam ।। sayonir lokam upa yāhi vidvān । tviṣiṃ palāvān apa tad vinaktu ।। dyaur evāsau pṛthivy antarikṣam ।
ā pyāyantāṃ punar ā yantu śūrpāt ।। ekarūpo bhavati saṃ samṛddhyām । grāvā śundhāti malaga iva vastrā ।। saṃ tvā dadhāmi pṛthivīṃ pṛthivyā ।
yajñāyudhair ājyenābhiṣiktāḥ ।। tanūḥ samānī vikṛtā ta eṣā । tena mā susror api tad vapāmi ।। indro rakṣād dakṣiṇato mahitvā ।
uttarāt tvā varuṇaḥ saṃ dadātai ।। bhūmyāḥ sacante urv antarikṣam । tā naḥ svargam abhi lokaṃ nayantu ।। divaṃ ca yanti pṛthivīṃ ca lokān ।
pātra āsiktāḥ pary agnir endhām ।। uta śukrāḥ śucayaś cāmṛtāsaḥ । āpaḥ śikṣantīḥ pravatā sunāthāḥ ।। phenam asyanti bahulaṃ ca bindum ।
-etais taṇḍulair bhavatā sam āpaḥ ।। prāṇāpānaiḥ saṃmitā oṣadhībhiḥ । sarvaṃ samāpaṃ śucayaḥ śucitvam ।। adbhir ātmānam api saṃ sṛjantām ।
mitās taṇḍulāḥ pradiśo yatīmāḥ ।। ahiṃsanta oṣadhīr dāntu parvam । -amanyutā vīrudho me bhavantu ।। priyaṃ hṛdaś cakṣuṣo valgv astu ।
imaṃ prāśnantu dakṣiṇato niṣadya ।। agniṣṭomaiḥ saṃmito devatābhiḥ । ehāḥ pari pātre dadṛśrām ।। acyutaṃ tvā devatāś cyāvayantu ।
udvāsayātaḥ pary agnidhānāt ।। svaḥ pakvenābhy aśnavātai । imaṃ svargaṃ gamayāntam agne ।। yāvantaḥ kāmāḥ samapūpuras tān ।
ekasmin pātre adhyuddharainam ।। ghṛtena pātram abhi ghārayedam । imaṃ devāso abhihiṃkarātha ।। uruḥ pṛthuś cāsamaḥ svargaḥ ।
devā enaṃ devatābhyaḥ pra yacchān ।। patir vā jāya uta tvat tiraḥ । saṃ rādhayantau saha lokam etam ।। asmāt putrāḥ pari ye saṃbabhūvuḥ ।
nābhiṃ janānāḥ śiśavaḥ samāyan ।। ghṛtena miśrā amṛtasya nābhayaḥ । śaratsu nidhipā abhīcchāt ।। anīśvarā abhitaḥ santv anye ।
tribhiḥ kāṇḍais trīn svargān arukṣat ।। kravyāt piśāca iha mā pra pāsta । ādityā no aṅgirasaḥ sacantām ।। ghṛtena miśraṃ prati vedayāmaḥ ।
-enaṃ svargaṃ sukṛtāv apītam ।। yasmāl lokāt parameṣṭhī samāpa । eṣa bhāgo aṅgiraso no atra ।। nidhiṃ śevadhiṃ pari dadhma etam ।
mā smānyasmā ut sṛjatā purā mat ।। na yan mitraiḥ samamamāna eti । anūnaṃ pātraṃ nihitaṃ no astu ।। mamed u karman karuṇe api jāyāḥ ।
anv ārabhethāṃ vaya uttarāvat ।। tamas te hantu yatame dviṣanti । pauruṣeyam apa mṛtyuṃ nudantu ।। ya oṣadhīḥ sacate yaś ca sindhūn ।
hiraṇyaṃ jyotir dadhato babhūva ।। -anagnāḥ sarve paśavo ye anye । amotaṃ vāso mukham odanasya ।। yad vā dhane anṛtaṃ vittakāmyā ।
tasmin sarvaṃ śamalaṃ sādayāthaḥ ।। tvaco dhūmaṃ pary ut pātayāsi । sayonir lokam upa yāhy etam ।। yathā vida ātmany anyavarṇāḥ ।
yā lohinī tāṃ te agnau juhomi ।। ādityāyeṣumata etaṃ pari dadhmaḥ । diṣṭaṃ no atra jarase ni neṣat । adhā pakvena saha saṃ bhavema ।।
vasubhya iṣumadbhya etam ।। mitrāyeṣumata etam ।। vātāyeṣumata etam ।। vīrudbhya iṣumatībhya etam ।।
aśanībhya iṣumatībhya etaṃ pari dadhmaḥ । diṣṭaṃ no atra jarase ni neṣat । athā pakvena saha saṃ bhavema ।। sūryeṇottabhitā dyauḥ ।
divi somo adhi śritaḥ ।। somena pṛthivī mahī । upasthe soma āhitaḥ ।। yat saṃpiṃṣanty oṣadhim ।
na tasyāśnāti pārthivaḥ ।। bārhataiḥ soma rakṣitaḥ । na te aśnāti pārthivaḥ ।। cakṣur āvad abhyañjanam ।
yad ayāt sūryā patim ।। nārāśaṃsī nyocanam । gāthayaiti pariṣkṛtā ।। kurīraṃ chanda opaśaḥ ।
-agnir āsīt purogavaḥ ।। aśvināstām ubhā varā । manasā savitādadāt ।। dyaur āsīd uta chadiḥ ।
yad ayāt sūryā patim ।। gāvau te sāmanāv aitām । divi panthāś carācaraḥ ।। vyāno akṣa āhataḥ ।
-ārohat prayatī patim ।। savitā yam avāsṛjat । phalgunīṣu vy uhyate ।। tricakreṇa vahatuṃ sūryāyāḥ ।
kva deṣṭrāya tasthathuḥ ।। vareyaṃ sūryām upa । putraḥ pitarāv avṛnīta pūṣā ।। brahmāṇa ṛtuthā viduḥ ।
tad addhātaya id viduḥ ।। yena tvābadhnāt savitā suśevāḥ । syonaṃ te astu sahapatnyai vadhu ।। subandhuṃ pativedanam ।
ito muñcantu māmutaḥ ।। subaddhām amutas karat । suputrā subhagāsati ।। -aśvinā tvā pra vahatāṃ rathena ।
vaśinī tvaṃ vidatham ā vadāsi ।। asmin gṛhe gārhapatyāya jāgṛhi । -atha jirvir vidatham ā vadāsi ।। dīrgham āyur vy aśnutam ।
modamānau sve gṛhe ।। śiśū krīḍantau pari yāto adhvaram । ṛtūṃr anyo vidadhaj jāyate navaḥ ।। ahnāṃ ketur uṣasām ety agram ।
pra candramās tirate dīrgham āyuḥ ।। brahmabhyo vi bhajā vasu । -ā jāyā viśate patim ।। kṛtyāsaktir vy ajyate ।
patir bandheṣu badhyate ।। ruśatī pāpayāmuyā । svam aṅgam abhyūrṇute ।। atho adhivikartanam ।
tāni brahmā tu śundhati ।। apāṣṭhavad viṣavan naitad attave । sa id vādhūyam arhati ।। brahmā vāsaḥ sumaṅgalam ।
yena jāyā na riṣyati ।। ṛtaṃ vadantām ṛtodyena । cāru sambhalo vadatu vācam etām ।। -imaṃ gāvaḥ prajayā vardhayātha ।
viśve devāḥ krann iha vo manāṃsi ।। ayaṃ devānāṃ na mināti bhāgam । asmai vo dhātā savitā suvāti ।। yebhiḥ sakhāyo yanti no vareyam ।
saṃ dhātā sṛjatu varcasā naḥ ।। aśvinā yena vā sūrā । tenemāṃ varcasāvatam ।। sūrāyāṃ ca yad āhitam ।
tenemāṃ varcasāvatam ।। yaṃ viprāsa īḍate adhvareṣu । yābhir indro vāvṛdhe vīryāvān ।। tānūdūṣim apa nudāmi ।
tam ud acāmi ।। avīraghnīr ud acantv āpaḥ । pratīkṣante śvaśuro devaraś ca ।। śaṃ methir bhavatu śaṃ yugasya tardma ।
śaṃ patyā tanvaṃ saṃ spṛśasva ।। sāmrājyaṃ suṣuve vṛṣā । patyur astaṃ paretya ।। samrājñy uta śvaśruvām ।
samrājñy uta devṛṣu ।। yā devīr antām̐ abhito adadanta । āyuṣmatīdaṃ pari dhatsva vāsaḥ ।। dīrghām anu prasitiṃ dīdhiyur naraḥ ।
mayaḥ patibhyo janaye pariṣvaje ।। aśmānaṃ devyāḥ pṛthivyā upasthe । dīrghaṃ ta āyuḥ savitā kṛṇotu ।। somo rājā suprajasaṃ kṛṇotu ।
patyā patnīṃ jaradaṣṭiṃ kṛṇotu ।। mayā patyā jaradaṣṭir yathāsaḥ । mahyaṃ tvādur gārhapatyāya devāḥ ।। hastaṃ jagrāha dakṣiṇam ।
mā vyathiṣṭhā mayā saha ।। savitā hastam agrahīt । aryamā hastam agrahīt । -ahaṃ gṛhapatis tava ।।
mahyaṃ tvādād bṛhaspatiḥ । saṃ jīva śaradaḥ śatam ।। bṛhaspateḥ praśiṣā kavīnām । sūryām iva pari dhattāṃ prajāyai ।।
jyotiṣmad idaṃ prati muñcasva vapuḥ । uṣā iva sūryasya saṃdṛśi ।। mitrāvaruṇā bhago aśvinobhā । imāṃ nārīṃ prajayā vardhayantu ।।
śīrṣe keṣām̐ akalpayat । patyā saṃ śobhayāmasi ।। jāyāṃ jijñāse manasā carantīm । ka imaṃ vidvān vi cacarta pāśam ।।
vedad it paśyan manasaḥ kulāyam । svayaṃ śrathnāno varuṇasya pāśam ।। yena tvābadhnāt savitā suśevaḥ । kṛṇomi tubhyaṃ sahapatnyai vadhu ।।
-imāṃ nārīṃ sukṛte dadhāta । bhago rājā pura etu prajānan ।। bhagas tatakṣa catvāry uṣpalāni । sā no astu sumaṅgalī ।।
prajāyai ca vareṇyam । sam agniṃ sam idhīmahi ।। hiraṇyavarṇaṃ suvṛtaṃ sucakram । syonaṃ patibhyo vahatuṃ kṛṇu tvam ।।
sthūne devakṛte pathi । syonaṃ kṛṇmo vadhūpatham ।। brahmāntato madhyato brahma sarvataḥ । śivā syonā patiloke vi rāja ।।
anuvāka ।। sūryāṃ vahatunā saha । agne prajayā saha ।। āyuṣā saha varcasā ।
jīvāti śaradaḥ śatam ।। gandharvas te aparaḥ patiḥ । turīyas te manuṣyajāḥ ।। gandharvo dadad agnaye ।
agnir mahyam atho imām ।। ny aśvinā hṛtsu kāmā araṃsata । priyā aryamṇo duryām̐ aśīmahi ।। rayiṃ dhehi sarvavīraṃ vacasyam ।
sthāṇuṃ pathiṣṭhām apa durmatiṃ hatam ।। śubhaspatī vahator yāto asmāt । kṣetravit pūrvo vi mṛdho nudasva ।। yāni kṣetrāṇi yā vanā ।
patye rakṣantu rakṣasaḥ ।। sugaṃ svastivāhanam । anyeṣāṃ vindate vasu ।। yayāśiṣā dampatī vāmam aśnutaḥ ।
eṣu vānaspatyeṣv adyādhi tasthuḥ । mā hiṃsiṣur vahatum uhyamānam ।। yakṣmā yanti janām̐ anu । nayantu yata āgatāḥ ।।
ya āsīdanti dampatī । apa drāntv arātayaḥ ।। aghoreṇa cakṣuṣā mitryeṇa । syonaṃ patibhyaḥ savitā kṛṇotu tat ।।
imaṃ dhātā lokam asyai viveda । prajāpatiḥ prajayā vardhayantu ।। tasyāṃ naro vapata bījam asyām । bibhratī dudhram ṛṣabhasya retaḥ ।।
viṣṇur iveha sarasvati । bhagasya sumatāv asat ।। āpo yoktrāṇi muñcantu । -aghnyau śūnam āratām ।।
śagmā suśevā suyamā gṛheṣu । -imam agniṃ gārhapatyaṃ sarpaya ।। syonā paśubhyaḥ sumanāḥ suvīrā । saṃ tvaidhiṣīmahi sumanasyamānā ।।
ahaṃ tveḍe abhibhūḥ svād gṛhāt । -uttiṣṭhārāte pra pata māti raṃsthāḥ ।। pūrvam agniṃ vadhūr iyam । pitṛbhyaś ca namas kuru ।।
-asyai nāryā upastire । bhagasya sumatāv asat ।। adhi carmaṇi rohite । imam agniṃ saparyatu ।।
carma copastṛṇīthana । yā kanyā vindate patim ।। eṣa devo hanti rakṣāṃsi sarvā । saṃpatnī prati bhūṣeha devān ।।
nānārūpāḥ paśavo jāyamānāḥ । sujyaiṣṭhyo bhavatu te putra eṣaḥ ।। suśeva patye śvaśurāya śambhūḥ । prajāvatī jaradaṣṭir yathāsaḥ ।।
imāṃ sameta paśyata । daurbhāgyena paretana ।। yāś ceha jaratīr api । -athāstaṃ vi paretana ।।
viśvā rūpāṇi bibhratam । bṛhate saubhagāya kam ।। -iha prajāṃ janaya patye asmai । jyotirugrā uṣasaḥ prati jāgaraḥ ।।
sam aspṛśanta tanvas tanūbhiḥ । prajāvatī patye śaṃ bhavāsi ।। viśvāvasuṃ namasā gīrbhir īḍe । sa te bhāgo januṣā tasya viddhi ।।
antarā havirdhānaṃ sūryaṃ ca । namas te gandharva rtunā kṛṇomi ।। namo bhāmāya cakṣuṣe ca kṛṇmaḥ । abhi jāyā apsarasaḥ parehi ।।
-ud ito gandharvam āvīvṛtāma । aganma vayaṃ pratiranta āyuḥ ।। pitā mātā ca retaso bhavāthaḥ । prajāṃ kṛṇvāthām iha modamānau ।।
ahorātrābhyāṃ sam anaktv aryamā । śaṃ no bhava dvipade śaṃ catuṣpade ।। yasyāṃ bījaṃ manuṣyā vapanti । yasyām uśantaḥ praharema śepaḥ ।।
pari ṣvajasva jāyāṃ sumanasyamānaḥ । dīrghaṃ vām āyuḥ savitā kṛṇotu ।। vāso vadhvaś ca vastram । bṛhaspate sākam indraś ca dattam ।।
vādhūyaṃ vadhvo vāso asyāḥ । sa id rakṣāṃsi talpyāni hanti ।। hasāmudau mahasā modamānau । jīvā uṣaso vibhātīḥ ।।
udāgāṃ jīva uṣaso vibhātīḥ । viśvasmād enasas pari ।। antisumne mahivrate । tā no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ ।।
mitrāya varuṇāya ca । tebhyo aham akaraṃ namaḥ ।। purā jatrubhya ātṛdaḥ । purūvasur niṣkartā vihṛtaṃ punaḥ ।।
nīlaṃ piśaṅgam uta lohitaṃ yat । asmin tāṃ sthāṇāv adhy ā sṛjāmi ।। yāvanto rājño varuṇasya pāśāḥ । -asmin tā sthāṇau prati muñcāmi sarvāḥ ।।
otavo ye ca tantavaḥ । tan mā syonam upa spṛṣāt ।। pitṛlokāt patiṃ yatīḥ । ava dīkṣām asṛkṣata svāhā ।।
viśve devā adhārayan । yat tenemāṃ saṃ sṛjāmasi ।। viśve devā adhārayan । yat tenemāṃ saṃ sṛjāmasi ।।
viśve devā adhārayan । yat tenemāṃ saṃ sṛjāmasi ।। viśve devā adhārayan । yat tenemāṃ saṃ sṛjāmasi ।।
viśve devā adhārayan । yat tenemāṃ saṃ sṛjāmasi ।। rodena kṛṇvaty agham । savitā ca pra muñcatām ।।
rodena kṛṇvanto agham । ।। rodena kṛṇvatīr agham । ।।
rodena kṛṇvantāv agham । ।। aghakṛdbhir aghaṃ kṛtam । savitā ca pra muñcatām ।।
pūlpāny āvapantikā । edhantāṃ pitaro mama ।। cakravākeva dampatī । dīrgham āyur vy aśnutām ।।
yad vopavāsane kṛtam । āsnāne tāṃ ni dadhmasi ।। vivāhe vahatau ca yat । mṛjmahe duritaṃ vayam ।।
kambale duritaṃ vayam । pra ṇa āyūṃṣi tāriṣan ।। sā me bibhāya vāsasaḥ । nīviṃ kṛṇuṣva mā vayaṃ riśāma ।।
kṛtrimaḥ kaṅkataḥ śatadan ya eṣaḥ । apa śīrṣaṇyaṃ likhāt ।। apa yakṣmaṃ ni dhattana । divaṃ mā prāpan morv antarikṣam ।
yamaṃ mā prāpat pitṝṃś ca sarvān ।। saṃ tvā nahyāmi payasauṣadhīnām । sā saṃnaddhā sanuhi vājam emam ।। dyaur ahaṃ pṛthivī tvam ।
prajām ā janayāvahai ।। putrīyanti sudānavaḥ । bṛhate vājasātaye ।। imaṃ vahatum āgaman ।
prajāvac charma yacchantu ।। prajām asyai draviṇaṃ ceha dattvā । virāḍ iyaṃ suprajā aty ajaiṣīt ।। dīrghāyutvāya śataśāradāya ।
dīrghaṃ ta āyuḥ savitā kṛṇotu ।। vi yoktrāṇi paricartanāni ca । śivā gṛhapatau bhava ।। syonā patye gṛhebhyaḥ ।
syonā puṣṭāyaiṣāṃ bhava ।। anuvāka ।। idaṃ rāṣṭraṃ pra viśa sūnṛtāvat । sa tvā rāṣṭrāya subhṛtaṃ pipartu ।।
viśa ā roha tvadyonayo yāḥ । catuṣpado dvipada ā veśayeha ।। indreṇa yujā pramṛṇīta śatrūn । triṣaptā marutaḥ svādusaṃmudaḥ ।।
garbho janīnāṃ januṣām upastham । gātuṃ prapaśyann iha rāṣṭram āhāḥ ।। mṛdho vy āsthad abhayaṃ te abhūt । kāmaṃ duhatām iha śakvarībhiḥ ।।
taṃ tantuṃ parameṣṭhī tatāna । adṛṃhad dyāvāpṛthivī balena ।। tena sva stabhitaṃ tena nākaḥ । tena devā amṛtam anv avindan ।।
samākṛṇvānaḥ praruho ruhaś ca । saṃ te rāṣṭram anaktu payasā ghṛtena ।। yābhir āpṛṇāsi divam antarikṣam । viśi rāṣṭre jāgṛhi rohitasya ।।
vatsaṃ gāyatrīm anu tā ihāguḥ । saṃmātā vatso abhy eti rohitaḥ ।। viśvā rūpāṇi janayan yuvā kaviḥ । tṛtīye cakre rajasi priyāṇi ।।
ghṛtāhutaḥ somapṛṣṭhaḥ suvīraḥ । gopoṣaṃ ca me vīrapoṣaṃ ca dhehi ।। rohitāya vācā śrotreṇa manasā juhomi । sa mā rohaiḥ sāmityai rohayāti ।।
tasmāt tejāṃsy upa memāny āguḥ । vocayaṃ te nābhiṃ bhuvanasyādhi majmani ।। ā kakud varcasā viśvavedaḥ । ā tvā ruroha rohito retasā saha ।।
divaṃ vaste ayam antarikṣam । svar lokān sam ānaśe ।। syonā yonis talpā suśevā । taṃ tvā parameṣṭhin pary agnir varcasā dadhātu ।।
vaiśvakarmaṇāḥ pari ye babhūvuḥ । pari rohito varcasā dadhātu ।। goṣṭhe no gā ramaya yoniṣu prajām । taṃ tvā parameṣṭhin pary ahaṃ varcasā dadhāmi ।।
varcasā mitrāvaruṇāv abhi tvā । -idaṃ rāṣṭraṃ kṛṇuhi sūnṛtāvat ।। pṛṣṭir vahati rohitaḥ । śubhā yāsi riṇann apaḥ ।
rohaṃ rohayottamam ।। sūriḥ suparṇā bṛhatī suvarcāḥ । tayā viśyāḥ pṛtanā abhi ṣyāma ।। -asau panthāḥ pṛṣatī yena yāti ।
tāṃ rakṣanti kavayo apramādam ।। sadā vahanty amṛtāḥ sukhaṃ ratham । divaṃ devaḥ pṛṣatīm ā viveṣa ।। pary agniṃ pari sūryaṃ babhūva ।
tasmād devā adhi sṛṣṭīḥ sṛjante ।। mahatas pary arṇavāt । sarvā ruroha rohito ruhaḥ ।। devānāṃ dhenur anapaspṛg eṣā ।
agniḥ pra stautu vi mṛdho nudasva ।। ghṛtavṛddho ghṛtāhutaḥ । sapatnān hantu ye mama ।। agnir yo naḥ pṛtanyati ।
sapatnān pra dahāmasi ।। vyathayā sajātam utpipānaṃ bṛhaspate । adhare padyantām apratimanyūyamānāḥ ।। -indra vajreṇa bāhumān ।
agnes tejobhir ā dade ।। sapatnān me 'dharān kṛṇu । te yantv adhamaṃ tamaḥ ।। ā ruroha śukrapṛṣṭho antarikṣam ।
brahma santaṃ brahmaṇā vardhayantu ।। rāṣṭraṃ ca roha draviṇaṃ ca roha । rohitena tanvaṃ saṃ spṛśasva ।। abhito yanti sūryam ।
rāṣṭraṃ dadhātu sumanasyamānaḥ ।। adhvagato harayas tvā vahanti । tiraḥ samudram ati rocase arṇavam ।। vasujiti gojiti saṃjiti saṃdhanājiti ।
voceyaṃ te nābhiṃ bhuvanasyādhi majmani ।। yaśāḥ paśūnām uta carṣaṇīnām । aham asmi saviteva cāruḥ ।। -iha san tāni paśyati ।
divi sūryaṃ vipaścitam ।। antaś caraty arṇave । taṃ viduḥ kavayaḥ pare ।। avaḥ pareṇa para ity ekā ।।
aṣṭāpadī navapadī babhūvuṣī । tyasyāḥ samudrā adhi vi kṣaranti ।। ut tvā yajñā brahmapūtā vahanti । ghṛtaṃ pibantaṃ harayas tvā vahanti ।।
yat ta ākramaṇaṃ divi । yat te sadhasthaṃ parame vyoman ।। sūrya āpo ati paśyati । ā ruroha divaṃ mahīm ।।
vedir bhūmir akalpata । himaṃ ghraṃsaṃ ca rohitaḥ ।। yūpān kṛtvā parvatān । rohitasya svarvidaḥ ।।
brahmaṇāgniḥ samāhitaḥ । tasmād yajño ajāyata ।। brahmavṛddho brahmahutaḥ । rohitasya svarvidaḥ ।।
satye anyaḥ samāhitaḥ । ।। yam indro brahmaṇaspatiḥ । rohitasya svarvidaḥ ।।
anuvāka ।। divaṃ kṛtvā dakṣiṇām । varṣeṇājyena rohitaḥ ।। vedir bhūmir akalpata ।
gīrbhir ūrdhvām̐ akalpayat ।। rohito bhūmim abravīt । yad bhūtaṃ yac ca bhāvyam ।। bhavyo ajāyata ।
rohitena rṣiṇābhṛtam ।। śukrā bhrājanta īrate । mahivratasya mīduṣaḥ ।। supakṣam āśuṃ patayantam arṇave ।
yo raśmibhir diśa ābhāti sarvāḥ ।। nānārūpe ahanī karṣi māyayā । yad eko viśvaṃ pari bhūma jāyase ।। vahanti yaṃ haritaḥ sapta bahvīḥ ।
taṃ tvā paśyema pariyantam ājim ।। sugena durgam ati yāhi śībham । ahorātre vimimāno yad eṣi ।। yenobhāv antau pariyāsi sadyaḥ ।
tam ā roha sukham āśvaśvam ।। syonaṃ suvahnim adhi tiṣṭha vājinam । śatam aśvā yadi vā sapta bahvīḥ ।। hiraṇyatvacaso bṛhatīr ayukta ।
vidhūya devas tamo divam āruhat ।। apāvṛk tamo abhi jyotir aśrait । adityāḥ putro bhuvanāni viśvā ।। prajāḥ sarvā vi paśyati ।
sarvāṃ lokān paribhūr bhrājamānaḥ ।। śiśū kundānā pari yāto arṇavam । hairaṇyair anyaṃ harito vahanti ।। sūryā māsāya kartave ।
svar bhūtāvacākaśat ।। vatsaḥ saṃmātarāv iva । brahma devā amī viduḥ ।। tat siṣāsati sūryaḥ ।
pūrvaś cāparaś ca yaḥ ।। tasmān nāpa cikitsati । devānāṃ nāva rundhate ।। devaṃ vahanti ketavaḥ ।
dṛśe viśvāya sūryam ।। nakṣatrā yanty aktubhiḥ । sūrāya viśvacakṣase ।। vi raśmayo janām̐ anu ।
bhrājanto agnayo yathā ।। jyotiṣkṛd asi sūrya । viśvam ā bhāsi rocanaḥ ।। pratyaṅṅ ud eṣi mānuṣīḥ ।
pratyaṅ viśvaṃ svar dṛśe ।। bhuraṇyantaṃ janām̐ anu । tvaṃ varuṇa paśyasi ।। ahar mimāno aktubhiḥ ।
paśyan janmāni sūrya ।। vahanti deva sūrya । śociṣkeśaṃ vicakṣaṇam ।। sūro rathasya naptyaḥ ।
tabhir yāti svayuktibhiḥ ।। siñcantīr ā caraṇyatha । abhi vatsaṃ na dhenavaḥ ।। pṛñcatīr varcasā priyaḥ ।
jātaṃ jātrīr yathā hṛdā ।। kīrtiṃ śremāṇam ā vahān । mahyam āyur ghṛtapriyaḥ ।। rohito divam ākramīt tapasā tapasvī ।
sa devānām adhipatir babhūva ।। viśvataspāṇir utaviśvataspṛdhaḥ । dyāvāpṛthivī janayan deva ekaḥ ।। dvipāt tripādam abhy eti paścāt ।
ta ekapadas tanvāṃ sam āsate ।। divi rūpaṃ kṛṇuṣe rocamānaḥ । viśvā āditya pravato vi bhāsi ।। baḍ āditya mahām̐ asi ।
tvam āditya mahām̐ asi ।। pṛthivyāṃ rocase rocase apsv antaḥ । devo devāsi mahiṣaḥ svarvit ।। āśur vipaścit patayan pataṅgaḥ ।
pra ketunā sahate viśvam ejat ।। araṃgamāsaḥ pravato rarāṇaḥ । viśvā āsthāt pradiśaḥ kalpamānaḥ ।। ārocayan rodasī antarikṣam ।
prāsya viśvā tirato vīryāṇi ।। jyotiṣmān pradiśaḥ sūrya udyan । viśvātārīd duritāni śukraḥ ।। cakṣur mitrasya varuṇasyāgneḥ ।
sūrya ātmā jagatas tasthuṣaś ca ।। madhye divas taraṇiṃ bhrājamāṇam । ajasraṃ jyotir yad avindad atriḥ ।। adityāḥ putraṃ nāthakāma upa yāmi bhītaḥ ।
mā riṣāma sumatau te syāma ।। kṛṇvāṇaḥ pārthivaṃ rajaḥ । kṛṇuṣe deva sūrya ।। harer haṃsasya pacataḥ svargam ।
saṃpaśyan yāti bhuvanāni viśvā ।। rohito agre prajāpatiḥ । rohito jyotir ucyate ।। rohito bhavyam ābharat ।
rohitaḥ svar ā bharat ।। rohito aty atapad divam । samudram anu saṃ carāt ।। rohito adhipatir divaḥ ।
sarvān lokān vi rakṣatu ।। ud ūhate raśmīn aṃśuṃ bṛhantam । hiraṇyayo haritaḥ ketur udyan ।। martyaḥ kṛṇute vīryāṇi ।
yat sarvān lokām̐ abhi yad vibhāti ।। ahorātrābhyāṃ mahiṣaḥ kalpamānaḥ । gātuvidaṃ havāmahe nāthakāmāḥ ।। gātur adabdhacakṣuḥ pari sarvaṃ babhūva ।
śivayā nas tanvā śarma yacchāt ।। jyotiṣā vibhrājan pari dyām antarikṣam । upā na āyuḥ pra tirād ariṣṭam ।। prati dhenum ivāyatīm uṣāsam ।
pra bhānavaḥ sisrate nākam accha ।। guhā bibharti na dadāti pitre । puraḥ paśyanti nihitam aratau ।। tveṣī bibharṣi mahiṣī jajāna ।
-apaśyaṃ jātaṃ yam asūta mātā ।। yasmai baliṃ devajanā haranti । guhā tiṣṭhanti vasunā samaktāḥ ।। navāntarikṣāṇi nava bhūmaya imāḥ ।
yasmād anyan na paraṃ kiṃ canāsti ।। na bhūtaṃ nota bhavyaṃ yad āsīt । sa evedam ā varīvarti bhūtam ।। somaṃ dipsanto ahyā nibāḍhāḥ ।
ko nidānaṃ ka ātmānam eṣām ।। ye dadante pañca diśaḥ sadhrīcīḥ । apāṃ netāraḥ katame ta āsan ।। antarikṣaṃ pary eko babhūva ।
sarvā diśo rakṣaty eka eṣām ।। anuvāka ।। vīyamāna eva sa prajāpatiṃ sam airayat ।। sa prajāpatir ātmani suparṇam apaśyat ।।
tad brahmābhavat tena prājāyata ।। sa devānām ekavratyo abhavat ।। sa dhenur ādhatta tad indradhanur abhavat ।। nīlam asyodaraṃ lohiny asya pṛṣṭiḥ ।।
lohitena dviṣantaṃ vidhyatīti brahmavādino vadanti ।। sa prācīṃ diśam anu vy acalat । taṃ bṛhac ca rathantaraṃ ca viśve ca devā ādityāś cānu vy acalan । ādityānāṃ ca priyaṃ dhāma bhavati ya evaṃ veda ।
-ā vṛścate ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ vrātyam upavadati ।। tasya prācyāṃ diśi । vāso ahar uṣṇīṣaṃ rātrī keśā haritau pravartau kalmalir maṇiḥ । ainaṃ yaśo gacchati ya evaṃ veda ।।
sa dakṣiṇāṃ diśam anu vy acalat । taṃ yajñāyāyajñiyaṃ ca vāmadevyaṃ ca yajñaś ca paśavaś cānu vy acalan । yajñāyāyajñiyasya ca vai sa vāmadevyasya ca yajñasya ca paśunāṃ ca । yajñāyāyajñiyāya ca vai sa vāmadevyāya ca yajñāya ca paśubhyaś ca ।।
tasya dakṣiṇāyāṃ diśi । ūṣāḥ pūṃścalī mantro māgadho । aho rātrī ca pariṣkandau ।। sa pratīcīṃ diśaṃ ।
taṃ vairūpaṃ ca vairājaṃ ca varuṇaś ca rājā paścānu vy acalan । vairūpasya ca vai sa vairājasya ca varuṇasya ca rājño apāṃ ca । vairūpāya ca vai sa vairājāya ca varuṇāya ca rājñedbhyaś ca ।। tasya pratīcyāṃ diśi ।
irāḥ puṃścalī haso māgadho । paurṇamāsī cāmāvāsyā ca pariṣkandau ।। sa udīcīṃ diśam anu vy acalat । taṃ śyaitaṃ ca naudhasaṃ ca somaś ca rājā sapta ṛṣayaś cānu vy acalan ।
sapta ṛṣīnāṃ ca priyaṃ dhāma bhavati ya । sapta ṛṣibhyaś cā vṛścate ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ vrātyam upavadati ।। tasyodīcyāṃ diśi । keśā haritau pravartau kalmalir maṇiḥ ।
ainaṃ kīrtir gacchaty ainaṃ yaśo gacchati ya ।। taṃ devā abruvan vrātya kiṃ nu tiṣṭhasīti । tasmā āsandīṃ sam abharan । pūrvau pādav āstāṃ varṣāś ca śarac cāparau ।
yajñāyajñiyaṃ ca vāmadevyaṃ ca tiraśce । ṛcaḥ prāñcas tantavo yajūṃṣi tīryañcaḥ । udgītho apaśrayantām asīdat । devajanāḥ pariṣkandā apsarasaḥ patnīr viśvāni bhūtāny upasadaḥ ।
