prajāvatīṣam akṣīyamāṇam । sā no devī suhavā śarma yacchatu ।। yā te vayaṃ cakṛmā yā tanūbhiḥ । yā goṣv oṣadhīṣv apsv antaḥ ।।
sukṣatratāvīratā yā sujātā । semaṃ yajñam avatu devajuṣṭam ।। yad ejati carati yac ca tiṣṭhati । -ānumate anu hi maṃsase naḥ ।।
anumate anumataṃ sudānu । iṣaṃ pinva viśvavāraṃ suvīram ।। prajābhyas tvā prajās tvānu prāṇantu prajā anu prāṇihi । śukraṃ te śukreṇa candraṃ candreṇāmṛtam amṛtena krīṇāmi ।।
prajāpater varṇaḥ । parameṇa paśunā krīyase ।। abhi tyaṃ devaṃ savitāram oṇyoḥ kavikratum । arcāmi satyasavaṃ ratnadhām abhi priyaṃ matim ।।
ūrdhvā yasyāmatir bhā adidyutat savīmani । hiraṇyapāṇir amimīta sukratuḥ kṛpā svaḥ ।। matir jyotir vidharmaṇi । bradhnaḥ samīcīr uṣasaḥ sam īrayāt ।।
svasare manyumattamāḥ । cite goḥ ।। ya eka id bhūr atithir janānām । taṃ vartanir anu vavṛta ekam it puru ।।
asmin yajñe suhavāṃ johavīmi । tasyai te devi haviṣā vidhema ।। havyā no asya haviṣaḥ śṛṇotu । rāyaspoṣaṃ cikituṣe dadhātu ।।
saṃ vo manāṃsi jānatām । mayi saṃjñānam astu vaḥ ।। anuvāka ।। viśve yad devā marutaḥ svarkāḥ ।
sarasvaty anumatir ni yacchāt ।। śarma yacchata dvipade catuṣpade । tad asmabhyaṃ śaṃ yor arapo dadhāta ।। saṃśitaṃ cit saṃtaraṃ saṃ śiśādhi ।
viśva enam anu madanti devāḥ ।। bṛhaspatir abhiśastyā amuñcata । devānām agne bhiṣajā śacībhiḥ ।। madyaṃ somaṃ pibataṃ dhṛtavratā ।
prati svasaram upa yāti pītaye ।। vṛṣṇaḥ somasya vṛṣaṇā vṛṣethām । āsadyāsmin barhiṣi mādayethām ।। -oru kṣayāya niṣ kṛdhi ।
pra pra yajñapatiṃ tira ।। uror vā viṣṇo maho antarikṣāt । -āprayaccha dakṣiṇād ota savyāt ।। yaḥ pārthivāni vimame rajāṃsi ।
vicakramāṇas tredhorugāyaḥ ।। mṛgo na bhīmaḥ kucaro giriṣṭhāḥ । adhikṣiyanti bhuvanāni viśvā ।। pātaṃ ghṛtasya guhyāni nāma ।
-opa vāṃ jihvā ghṛtam ā caraṇyāt ।। vītaṃ ghṛtasya guhyā juṣāṇā । prati vāṃ jihvā ghṛtam uc caraṇyāt ।। bhindhīdaṃ divyaṃ nabhaḥ ।
īśāno vi ṣyā bilam ।। gṛṇāno daivyaṃ sahaḥ । devo devānāṃ sakhyā juṣāṇaḥ ।। dhātā vidhartā bhuvaneṣv eṣu ।
nemenāmuṣmai viṣuvān nv edhi ।। -īdaṃ śṛṇotu yad ahaṃ bravīmi । nemenāmuṣmai viṣuvān nv edhi ।। atraivainaṃ sarva vi vṛśca ।
nemenāmuṣmai viṣuvān nv edhi ।। asmin me have havyo yathāsaḥ । -āmuṃ chinatti varuṇasya pāśāt ।। upārima caraṇair jātavedaḥ ।
śubhe sakhibhyo amṛtatvam asmān ।। agne adhyakṣo na ehi pāhi no duritāt pāhi duṣvapnyāt । āsanyād anyād yakṣmān naḥ pāhi ।। tviṣir asi tviṣivanto bhūyāsma ।
prajāvanto varcasvinaḥ ।। kṣīraṃ bharathodhabhiḥ । payo harāmi vīrudhā ।। adbhyaḥ saṃbharathā madhu ।
kṣīraṃ harāmy oṣadhyā ।। śayānam akasvalam । pary asmān varuṇo dadhat ।। ghorāṃ vācaṃ mithuyānubruvanti ।
duryoṇam asmat pari te harantu ।। rathīva patyai na janayat purohitaḥ । adhaspadaṃ kṛṇutāṃ ye pṛtanyavaḥ ।। tava dyumnāny uttamāni santu ।
śatrūyatām abhi tiṣṭhā mahāṃsi ।। imaṃ no yajñam upa yāhi vidvān । śatrūyatām ā bharā bhojanāni ।। praty ajātāñ jātavedo nudasva ।
śarma no yaccha trivarūtham udbhit ।। praty ajātāñ jātavedaḥ śṛṇīhi । -ānu tvā devā vasavo madantām ।। sapatno votpipāno bṛhaspate ।
yathendrāham uttamaś cetayāni ।। mama vaśam upa tiṣṭhantu sarve । vasor madhye dīdihi jātavedaḥ ।। jāsayotpipānaṃ sapatnam ।
viśvā dveṣāṃsy abhito ni mṛḍḍhi ।। viśas tvā sarvā balihṛta upāsatām । sve kṣetre saviteva vi rāja ।। sarasvantaṃ puṣṭipatiṃ rayīṇām ।
iha huvema sadanaṃ rayīṇām ।। yasya vrata upatiṣṭhanta āpaḥ । taṃ sarasvantam avase huvema ।। madhumanto ghṛtaścutaḥ ।
tebhir no avitā bhuvaḥ ।। apāṃ garbhaṃ vṛṣabham oṣadhīnām । sarasvantaṃ rayiṣṭhāṃ sādayeha ।। ātmā devānām uta viśvarūpaḥ ।
yā anyatreha tās te svadhito gṛṇantu ।। sahasrapāc chatayonir vayodhāḥ । asmākam astu pitṛṣu svadhāvat ।। śyeno nṛcakṣā avasānadarśaḥ ।
-īndreṇa sakhyā śiva ā jagāma ।। urujyotir avidāmā namobhiḥ । yatra somaḥ sadam it tatra bhadram ।। ud vayam ity ekā ।।
patir viśvasya bhuvanasya rājati । patnīvān agna iha yāhi somam ।। prāṇāpānau sayujeha stam । ta enaṃ svasti jarase nayantu ।।
apānaḥ prāṇo ya u te paretaḥ । tad ātmani punar ā veśayāmi ।। mā tvāpāno avahāya parā gāt । agniṣ ṭe gopā adhipā vasiṣṭhaḥ ।।
śṛṇotu naḥ subhagā bodhatu tmanā । dadātu vīraṃ śatadāyam ukthyam ।। yābhir dadāti dāśuṣe vasūni । sahasrapoṣaṃ subhage rarāṇā ।।
yā guṅgūr yā sarasvatī । varuṇānīṃ svastaye ।। suṣumā bahusūvarī । sinīvālyai juhotana ।।
yā devānām asi svasā । prajāṃ devi didiḍḍhi naḥ ।। sahasrastutām abhi yantu devīḥ । patiṃ devi rādhasā codayasva ।।
anuvāka ।। upa hvaya iti tisraḥ ।। ।। ।।
sūyavasād bhagavatīty ekā ।। patnīvanto namasyaṃ namasyān । sakhet sakhyur nimiṣi rakṣamāṇāḥ ।। tapto vāṃ gharma ā gatam ।
dasrā vadanti kāravaḥ ।। tapto gharmo duhyate vām iṣe madhu । havāmahe sadhamādeṣu kāravaḥ ।। ayaṃ so aśvinā vāṃ bhāga ā gatam ।
taptaṃ gharmaṃ pibataṃ rocane divaḥ ।। pra vām adhvaryuś carati payasvān । vītaṃ pātaṃ payasa usriyāyāḥ ।। ā gharme siñca paya usriyāyāḥ ।
anu dyāvāpṛthivī supraṇītiḥ ।। yo aśvinoś camaso devapānaḥ । gandharvasya praty āsnā rihanti ।। ya ātasthedaṃ savanaṃ juṣāṇāḥ ।
astaṃ gharmaṃ tam udātiṣṭhatānu ।। sumṛḍīkā sarasvati । mā te yuyoma saṃdṛśaḥ ।। camasena bṛhaspatiḥ ।
indra gīrbhir na ā bhara ।। saṃ mā siñcantu maruta ity ekā ।। yasyāḥ pade punate devayantaḥ । -opa yajñam asthita vaiśvadevī ।।
drapsaś caskandety ekā ।। bāhucyuto dhiṣaṇāyā upasthāt । taṃ te juhomi manasā vaṣaṭkṛtam ।। drapsaḥ patito viśvayaḥ pariśrutaḥ ।
saṃ taṃ siñcatu rādhase ।। dhānāsomaḥ parivāpaḥ karambhaḥ । saṃ taṃ siñcatu varcase ।। payasvan māmakaṃ vaca ity ekā ।।
āyuṣ ṭe viśvato dadhat । parā yakṣmaṃ suvāmi te ।। viśām urukṣitīnām । īrṣyāyā nāma bheṣajam ।।
-īrṣyāyā nāma bheṣajam । tad aśnā saṃgṛbhāyikam ।। dāvasya dahato yathā । udnāgnim iva vāraye ।।
manyuṃ te hṛdayād adhi । tatro enāṃ ni dadhmasi ।। pṛdākor adhi saṃbhṛtam । iyaṃ vīrud adūduṣat ।।
atho maśakajambhanī ।। tatas tvā nir ṇayāmasi । maśakasyārasaṃ viṣam ।। mukhāny eṣāṃ vṛjinā kṛṇoṣi ।
iṣīkām iva saṃ namaḥ ।। hiraṇyam aśvam uta gām ajām avim । agniṣ ṭad viśvād agadaṃ kṛṇotu ।। yācamānasya vadato vicukṣubhe ।
sarasvatī tad ā pṛṇād ghṛtena ।। siṣāsanto balim agne carantaḥ । vaiśvānaraḥ prati havyā gṛbhāya ।। vīkṣāyāḥ pāśād uta śakvarīṇām ।
dātṝṇāṃ dānaṃ bhunajāmahai vayam ।। adāt savitedam । priyo mitro adād idam ।। -āpa bādhe pṛtanyataḥ ।
adhare santu śatravaḥ ।। hato vṛtrāṇy aprati । ugrā hi vṛtrahantamā ।। purodhāyai havāmahe ।
tau no mṛḍāta īdṛśe ।। yāv ātasthatur bhuvanā juṣāṇā । agnim indraṃ vṛtrahaṇā huvema ।। yau vīryair vīratamā śacībhiḥ ।
viṣṇum agan varuṇaṃ pūrvahūtiḥ ।। praririce pradivi rocanāyām । viṣṇum agan varuṇaṃ pūrvahūtiḥ ।। prajām ati vi ca caṣṭe śacībhiḥ ।
viṣṇum agan varuṇaṃ pūrvahūtiḥ ।। na parā jigye kataraś canaiva vām । tredhā sahasraṃ vi tad airayethām ।। yac carāmasi pāpayā ।
duritāt pāntu viśvataḥ ।। duṣvapnyaṃ durjīvitam ity ekā ।। mukhena nirṛte tava । havyavāḍ ghṛtasūdanaḥ ।।
niṣpatya tata ānaśe । duritāt pāntu viśvataḥ ।। nirṛtyāṃ viśvā duritāni mṛjmahe । varuṇo rājā savitā pavitraiḥ ।।
yātudhānanibādhitaḥ । tam u syonaṃ kṛṇomi te ।। devebhyas pari nirhataḥ । vi te pāśāṃś cṛtāmasi ।।
ud amuṃ chindhi tṛṣṭike । sarvasmai śepyāvate ।। viṣā viṣātaky asi । ṛṣabheṇa vaśeva ।।
ā dade hṛdayād adhi । ā puṃso yat titṛpsasi ।। mayi dyumnaṃ mayi tviṣiḥ । ahaṃ bhūyāsam uttamaḥ ।।
anuvāka ।। yuktvā śapatho ratham । vṛka ivāvimato gṛham ।। hradam agnir iva dahan ।
divyā vṛkṣam ivāśaniḥ ।। śapato yaś ca naḥ śapāt । ā mūlād anu śuṣyatu ।। yaḥ suhārt tena naḥ saha ।
pṛṣṭīr api śṛṇīmasi ।। aghāyur yaś ca naḥ śapāt । taṃ praty asyāmi mṛtyave ।। prānudhyāḥ pro aśastayaḥ ।
somo hantu durasyatīḥ ।। naśyetaḥ prāmutaḥ pata । yaṃ dviṣmas tasmin tvā sṛjāmaḥ ।। -ādhicaskanda vandaneva vṛkṣam ।
hiraṇyahasto vasu no rarāṇaḥ ।। nir hastayor varuṇo mitro aryamā । pra ṇaḥ suvāt savitā saubhagāya ।। sākaṃ martyasya januṣeha jātāḥ ।
śivāsmabhyaṃ jātavedo ni yaccha ।। yad vā keśeṣu praticakṣaṇe vā । pra tvā suvāt savitā saubhagāya ।। nir arātiṃ suvāmasi ।
rāyaspoṣam ihā suva ।। cakṣūṃṣīva sūryaṃ saṃ caranti । śveto vājī jāyate agre ahnām ।। adhi kṣami viṣurūpaṃ yad asti ।
codad rādha upastutaś cid arvāk ।। patyāṃ niviṣṭā yadi vā gha patnyām । tā ito haviṣā nir yajāmaḥ ।। prajāṃ lakṣmīr yadi vā te babhasti ।
nirhūya pra dadhmāv adhi dūram asmat ।। goṣedhāṃ vidhamām uta । brahmaṇā tā anīnaśam ।। uta cchidrām utāraṇīm ।
vyāghrīṃ nāśayāmasi ।। vibādhām uta hiṃsatīm । pra tā dhamāmi lakṣmyaḥ ।। yeṣantīṃ tapanīm uta ।
brahmaṇā tā anīnaśam ।। saṃpibantīṃ nyakvarīm । pra tā dhamāmi lakṣmyaḥ ।। yā te lakṣmīḥ sarvā samaktā ।
-āpaḥ śundhantu bṛhate raṇāya ।। -āpatighnīṃ bṛhaspate । asyai tāḥ savitaḥ suva ।। yā hastayo stanayor yopapakṣayoḥ ।
sarvās tā ati krāma ghorāḥ ।। pārṣṇibhyāṃ prapadābhyām । yāḥ pāpīs tā anīnaśan ।। apa hastayor varuṇo mitro aryamā ।
pra ṇaḥ suvāt savitā saubhagāya ।। khile gā aditīr iva । yāḥ pāpīs tā anīnaśan ।। sahamānā sahasvatī ।
tā ihā veśayāmasi ।। -ānyā anyāṃ jinvati bhadrapāpīḥ । bhadrā subhadrām api saubhagāya? ।। tāsāṃ rājñī babhūvitha ।
bhadreṇābhi sacasva naḥ ।। vātāt paśubhyo adhy oṣadhībhyaḥ । sā brahmaṇā pracyutā dūram etu ।। hiraṇyavarcasena ca ।
bhago mā tena jinvatu ।। tato lakṣmīr ny adadhur martyeṣu । śivā asyai jātavedo ni yaccha ।। gṛhebhyas tvā nudate yā vyāḍā ।
-ot taremāḥ srotyāḥ sapta sākam ।। saṃpibantīṃ nyakvarīm । brahmaṇā tā anīnaśam ।। jayantīm aparājitām ।
tā asyai savitaḥ suva ।। sam alapsata lakṣmyaḥ । parā pāpīr ajeṣata ।। lakṣmīṇām adhipā asi ।
devajā hi babhūvitha ।। prajāpater duhitarau sacetasau । antar vadāni hṛdaye janānām ।। prajāpater duhitaraḥ pracetasaḥ ।
antar vadāni hṛdaye janānām ।। māṃ prāṇantam anu prāṇantu sarve । mayi devā ekavṛto bhavantu ।। bṛhaspatir vācaḥ somo rājā sabhāyāḥ ।
indro vo dṛśe bhavāmi ।। subhadrāsi sarasvati । te me santu suvācasaḥ ।। viṣūcīr vāca īrate ।
mahyaṃ śivatamāḥ kṛdhi ।। ahaṃ vijñānam ā dade । indro yo gāyatām iva ।। uttamā hi babhūvitha ।
gandharvaḥ śaradaḥ śatam ।। ahaṃ bhūyāsam uttamaḥ । dviṣantam ava dhūnve ।। samudrasya bilaṃ yathā ।
mūtraṃ te tanvas pari ।। yathā samudra ejati । bahir jarāyuṇā saha ।। śive me dyāvāpṛthivī abhūtām ।
na vai tvā dviṣmo abhayaṃ no astu ।। bhadrāc chreyo abhi no neṣa vasyaḥ । dvipāc catuṣpān mayy astu puṣṭam ।। viśvā rūpāṇy āviśan ।
sakhā suśeva edhi naḥ ।। -ogro virājann apa vṛṅkṣva śatrūn । virājāṃ jīvāc charadaḥ śatāni ।। dampatyoḥ kṛṇutaṃ dīrgham āyuḥ ।
-īdaṃ kulāyam upasaṃviśāti ।। vāyuś ca mā pavamānaḥ punītām ।। tava satyaṃ vivācanam । semaṃ janaya pūruṣam ।।
mādhuntasya nikṛtvanaḥ । tena tvon mādayāmasi ।। pūrve patatam aśvibhyām । udnevāgnim avīvare ।।
mā riphanto vi gātana । yuṣmān anv etu kilbiṣam ।। iha cakṣur upa hvaye । ihendriyaṃ dadhātana ।।
imaṃ vatsaṃ vanād iyam । vatso devi mamāra te ।। nijavatseva dohasva । saṃvananasya veda te ।।
eṣa te aghnye vatsas taṃ vāñcha । tāṃ satyoktiṃ brūmaḥ ।। sā vāmenāṅkasā nyetya । imāṃ gāṃ vānayatu svāhā ।।
anuvāka ।। bahūny ati yojanā । na dṛṣṭo duṣkṛtaṃ karat ।। vatsasya śepyām iva ।
kṛṣṇo viṣāṇavām̐ iva ।। sacchavayaḥ sanābhayaḥ । vatsā ud rihatāṃ mithaḥ ।। savitā tvotāparaḥ ।
tṛtīyam aśvinā tvāghnye vāñcha ।। -ā nayatu bṛhaspatiḥ । tam asyai dhehy oṣadhe ।। indraṃ vayam anurādham ity ekā ।।
anu tvā vayam emasi । svasti nayatāṃ pathā ।। bṛhaspatiḥ puraetā te astu । śūdrāc ca na āryāc ca ।।
uṣṭārā uta pīlvā । sam īrmān sam u sakthyaḥ ।। gardabhā kṣipitā iva । mayīdaṃ sthāpayāmasi ।।
saṃ mā pṛthivyā saṃ mauṣadhībhiḥ । bhagena varcasā sican ।। varco me mitrāvaruṇety ekā ।। yābhyāṃ karmāṇi kṛṇvate ।
yajñaṃ deveṣu yacchatām ।। cakṣuḥ prāṇam atho balam । -āyuṣmantaḥ sumedhasaḥ ।। jagaddhātrī ca rakṣatam ।
avinaṣṭam avihrutam ।। sākaṃ jajñire agraśaḥ । kṛṣṇāḥ keśā bhavantu me ।। kṛṣṇān keśān sarasvati ।
kṛṇutaṃ puṣkarasrajā ।। purastād avatiṣṭhati । tan me 'bravīt tvaṣṭā viriṣṭabheṣajam ।। viśvabheṣajyā kṛtam ।
niṣkṛtir nāma vā asi ।। saṃ yoniṃ saṃ gavīnyau । saṃ garbhaṃ ca jarāyu ca ।। hṛdayasthaṃ jarāyu te ।
-ād gaccha yamasādanam ।। vi yoniṃ vi gavīnyau । vi garbhaṃ ca jarāyu ca ।। anusota jarāyu te ।
yathā jīvāsi bhadrayā ।। vi yona āsyaṃ sṛja । garbho gavīnyor adhi ।। tau viṣvañcau vyākuru ।
sa viṣvañcau vy asyatu ।। manaś ca hṛdayaṃ ca vām । śaśvatībhyaḥ samābhyaḥ ।। svāṃ yonim apīhi ।
mā parā seci me payaḥ ।। parāpapātāsmṛtam । tan mā pyāyatāṃ punaḥ ।। dhartā keśām̐ adhārayat ।
dhātā tvaṣṭā tvaci keśām̐ acīkl̥pat ।। divyeṣu devi dhāmasu । pra ṇa āyūṃṣi tāriṣaḥ ।। goṣv aśveṣu yan madhu ।
mukham aṅdhi sarasvati varcasā ।। tvāṃ ca māṃ cāntarāyati । duritāni ca mṛjmahe ।। agniṃ tiṣṭhasy antarā ।
na cchāyāṃ karavo aparam ।। brahmāṇo ghnantu menyā । agniṃ tiṣṭhaty antarā ।। -āgniṃ tiṣṭhaty antarā ।
sa rudrasyāstv ākhaṇaḥ ।। mṛtyur vi kramatām adhi । mṛtyoḥ pāśair bandhair avimokyaiḥ ।। keśin grāmaṃ na ā vada ।
-olūkācchā vadāmasi ।। parācīm anu saṃvatam । niyastaṃ praticākaśam ।। yaṃ dviṣmas tam ito naya ।
ākhus te mūṣiked bhāgaḥ ।। dhītavatsam anaṣṭagum । śune catuṣpadāṃ vada ।। punar indraḥ punar bhagaḥ ।
āyur jīvitavā aduḥ ।। mātra tiṣṭho abhicākaśat । -āthāsmābhiḥ sahāsasi ।। na va ihāsti nyañcanam ।
tad anuvadhvaṃ sudatīr ahinas tat ।। viṣṭhitāḥ pṛthivīm anu । ahaṃ bhūyāsam uttamaḥ ।। āhitāḥ pṛthivīm anu ।
sa no jīvātave kṛdhi ।। -āgnayaś ca nihavā nāma । tebhyo vo namo na vo havam emi । sa vo havam etu ।।
sthiravīrāv aparāvītagū । vayaṃ vidyāma guhyaṃ nāma gavām ।। viśve devāḥ padavāyāḥ santv āsām । indrajyeṣṭhāḥ punar ā vartayantu ।।
-āśvinā māṃ vahatam āśvaśvā । yathobhayebhyaś cāru samitim ā vadāni ।। cāru saṃ kāśa no nṛbhiḥ । jigīvām̐ aparājitaḥ ।।
vratater iva guṣpitam । madhu tad indrasya vibhajāvahai ।। varuṇasya vratena te । strīṣu cāso anāvayāḥ ।।
bhaṅgurasya nitodinaḥ । yad ātataṃ ni tat tanu ।। klībaṃ tvā vīrudhākaram । strīṣv apyākṛtaś cara ।।
dadhātv indreṇa medinā । ā no vahantu sindhavaḥ ।। medam indro dadhātu me । -ā dhattāṃ puṣkarasrajā ।।
aṣṭhīvantā uraś ca me । medam indro dadhātu me ।। sarvān keśān vṛhāmi te । yathāsat samaraṃ samam ।।
anuvāka ।। sapta sūryasya raśmayaḥ । tās te śalyam acucyavuḥ ।। iha prasakto vi cayat kṛtaṃ naḥ ।
pradakṣiṇaṃ marutāṃ stomam ṛdhyām ।। pitā putrebhyo apy avīvatad v ṛtā । ubhe yatete ubhe asya puṣyataḥ ।। parśur vediḥ paraśur naḥ svastiḥ ।
te devāso havir idaṃ juṣadhvam ।। yuvānam āhutīvṛdham । aganma bibhrato namaḥ ।। sahasraṃ dhamanīr uta ।
aśmanā bilam apy adhām ।। māṃpaśyam abhirorudam । -īndrāṇī kevalaṃ patim ।। anīkaṃ nau samañjanam ।
mana in nau sahāsati ।। -erṣyāṃ vy amīmadam । tam u te śamayāmasi ।। ahā viśvā sumanā dīdhyo naḥ ।
prajāvanta upa sadema sarve ।। mā vo vidyut taran mota senā । parivṛjya vadhaṃ gohanaṃ carantu ।। devebhir eta ।
ghṛtenā naḥ sam ukṣata ।। atho yā upapakṣiyāḥ । tā ito nāśayāmasi ।। marutas taj jujuṣṭana ।
yuṣmākotī riśādasaḥ ।। tiraś cittāni vasavo jighāṃsāt । tapiṣṭhena tapasā hantanā tam ।। urukṣayāḥ sagaṇā mānuṣebhyaḥ ।
sāṃtapanā matsarā mādayiṣṇavaḥ ।। vṛtrahā śūra samare vasūnām । rayiṣṭhāno rayim asmāsu dhehi ।। -āsmai kṣatrāṇi dhārayantam agne ।
premaṃ voco havirdāṃ devatāsu ।। vi yoktraṃ vi niyojanam । ihaiva tvam ajasra edhy agne ।। viśvā rūpāṇi mahinā jajāna ।
vayaṃ syāma patayo rayīṇām ।। amāvāsye saṃvasanto mahitvā । rayiṃ no dhehi subhage suvīram ।। ghṛtena tvā manur adyā sam īdhe ।
ghṛtaṃ tubhyaṃ duhrate gāvo agre ।। saha kṣatreṇa varcasā balena । svāhā mayy agniḥ ।। gṛho mito hiraṇyayaḥ ।
sarvā dhāmāni no muceḥ ।। ito varuṇa no muceḥ ।। varuṇeti yad ūcima । tato varuṇa no muceḥ ।।
ya oṣadhīr vīrudha āviveśa । tasmai rudrāya namo astv adya ।। apehy arir asy arir vā asi । ahim evābhy apehi taṃ jahi ।।
ugraṃ huvema paramāt sadhasthāt । kṣāsad devo ati duritāny agniḥ ।। tad brāhmaṇaṃ punar asmān upaitu ।। śaṃ me tapatu sūryaḥ ।
śam uṣā me vy ucchatu ।। yamaṃ rājānam avasānam arcata । tasmai lokaṃ kṛṇuta yāvatsabandhu ।। devair dattam asūriyaṃ ca saṃbhṛtam ।
mṛtyuṃ praty auhan padayopanena ।। agamad vasatiṃ vayaḥ । sthāman vṛkkāv arīramam ।। āgnidhānāny agnayaḥ ।
utsaktabheṣajam asi ।। -āntas tiṣṭhati tejanam । muñjas tiṣṭhatiy antarā ।। asthād vāto vanacyavaḥ ।
tiṣṭhād rogo ayaṃ tava ।। sahasraṃ saṃbhṛtāni ca । vasiṣṭhaṃ roganāśanam ।। hotaś cikitvann avṛṇīmahīha ।
prajānan vidvān upa yāhi somam ।। saṃ sūribhir harivan saṃ svastyā । saṃ brahmaṇā devakṛtaṃ yad asti ।। saṃ varcasety ekā ।।
prastareṣṭhā barhiṣadaś ca devāḥ । svāhā devā amṛtā mādayantām ।। tān preraya punar agne sve sadhasthe । asmai dhatta vasavo vasūni ।।
uttarāṃ vedim apy etu vediḥ । devā yakṣīṣṭa punar uttarāvat ।। yajñapatiṃ gaccha । svāṃ yoniṃ gaccha svāhā ।।
eṣa te yajño yajamāna sahasūktanamovākaḥ । suvīraḥ svāhā ।। manasaspata imaṃ deva yajñam । svāhā vāci svāhā vāte dhāḥ svāhā ।।
vaṣaḍ ḍhutebhyaḥ । devā gātuvido gātuṃ vittvā gātum ita svāhā ।। sam indreṇa vasubhiḥ saṃ marudbhiḥ । indraṃ gacchatu yat svāhā ।।
prajāṃ cakṣur atho balam । saṃ nahye amṛtāya kam ।। ud aṃśena patividye bibheda । upastha indraṃ sthaviraṃ pipartu ।।
-āditir viśvarūpā sūryatvak । tasyai ta enā haviṣā vidhema ।। tvarī prāṣāṭ tūrtam upacarantīm । tvarikas tvayiṣamesa tvā bhadre ।।
pāpāt svapnād abhūtyāḥ । parā svapnamukhāḥ śucaḥ ।। na prātar adhigamyate । nahi tad dṛśyate divā ।।
anuvāka ।। āyadāyat prati gṛhṇāmy annam । syonam asmabhyaṃ madhumat kṛṇotu ।। indrāya dhriyase ।
pūṣā te prāśitā ।। pāhi gāḥ pāhi yat tanūkṛtam । tāv asmān pāto aṃhasaḥ ।। svarbhānuś ca svarjyotiś ca ।
agneṣ ṭvā vaiśvānarasya tvāsyena prāśnāmi ।। svarbhānuś ca mārutaḥ । mo vayaṃ prajayā dhanena ।। anādhṛṣyaśavasaḥ ।
bhakṣaṃ kriyāsma ।। tvāṃ tam ahaṃ nir hvaye punaḥ । ūrvor astu me javaḥ ।। pṛthivyā adhy udbhṛtam ।
akṣyāmayabheṣajam asy ātharvaṇam ।। catasro bhūmyā diśaḥ । jīvena bhunajāmahai ।। tejane naṣṭavedanam ।
punar asmā aśvinā naṣṭam ājatam ।। yadi vānyata ābhṛtaḥ । devīr āpa imā mama ।। dṛśāmbasyota garmutaḥ ।
āśūnāṃ dhāvatām iva ।। vadha iva prasarpati । kṛkavākuś ca jakṣatu ।। nitatnir bhūmyām adhi ।
mithunā sam avīvanat ।। pari tvāgāṃ sahīyasā । suparṇān nikarīyasā ।। niraṣṭhaviṣam asmṛtam ।
punar me jaṭhare dhattām ।। duhitāsi prajāpateḥ । upa tvā hvaya upa mā hvayasva । nariṣṭā nāma vā asi ।।
kūlād adhi praskandati । bhagaṃ jayantī dhanaṃ jayantī ।। gandharvasyānuśāsanam । etat te pativedanam ।।
pāṭā kumbhīṃ gadohanīm । vadhūṃ kṛṇotu viśvataḥ ।। asmad iccha puruṣaṃ kaṃ cid eva । veda te takman pitaraṃ veda mātaram ।।
śamīvān ābhiśokiḥ । harṣaṇo jāñjabhiḥ ।। yaṃ tvam aṃśena bhejiṣe । na mām abhyetum arhasi ।।
kiḥkiśo nāma te pitā । śimidā nāma te svasā ।। girau te māhiṣo gṛhaḥ । nāmlāte ni krandayiṣyati ।।
sarvasya dūto abhiśastipāḥ । tad viṣasyāpa siñcatu ।। iṣṭaṃ haridruparṇyam । yathā jīvāsi bhadrayā ।।
yunajmi prathamasya ca । -oduhya prati dhāvatāt ।। yasta āsann avarūḍha eṣaḥ । sa no mā hiṃsīj jyāyaso mā kanīyasaḥ ।।
mā no hiṃsīj jyāyaso mā kanīyasaḥ । taṃ te dantaḥ sacatāṃ ghora eṣaḥ ।। durhārde dantaṃ pra hiṇomi ghoram । śivo asmabhyaṃ sumanā astv eṣaḥ ।।
śivo mahyaṃ kurvate danto astu । śivo mahyaṃ nabhasī rodasī stām ।। araṃkṛd vahator asi । taṃ tena prati gṛhṇāmi ।।
bṛhan mimāya jamadagnidattā । śravo deveṣv amṛtam ajuryam ।। adhi śravaḥ pāñcajanyāsu kṛṣṭiṣu । yāṃ me pulasti jamadagnayo daduḥ ।।
ni padaś caturo jahi । śaphām̐ urasi vādaya ।। padāvartaya goduham । tān viṣūco vi nāśaya ।।
ni kulpham abhinṛtyati । sarvān sākam ud ardaya ।। syandantām asya dhenavaḥ । yo asmān nāpacāyati ।।
vyāghrasya yathā manaḥ । yo asmān nāpacāyati ।। vīrudhāṃ balavattamaḥ । sarvāḥ syandaya gā imāḥ ।।
aranturathantu । pṛthivyām astu yad dharaḥ ।। akṛd aśvataro hariḥ । bhasan nadatv āsicā ।।
evā nadati te bhasat । -aitat paśyābhidarśanam ।। ut sūryam ud rātrim ud ahaḥ ।। antarikṣāya mṛtyave ।
mā mā hiṃsiṣur īśvarāḥ ।। payo devīr ahṛṣata । cakṣuṣe ca balāya ca । mayi tyā devatāḥ punaḥ ।।
tvaṃ devi tatarpitha । yuṣmad apsarasas pari ।। vayam ud apsarasas pari । prajām ā pyāyāmahe ।।
jāgrataḥ svapataś ca yat । ā siñcantu tanū adhi ।। yad oṣadhīr vyasarad yad āpaḥ । asmāṃs tat sacatāṃ payaḥ ।।
aśvā adhodhuraṃ yathā । vi vaster āsyaṃ sṛja ।। viṣitaṃ te vastibilam ity ekā ।। śukraṃ jyotir amartyam ।
tan naḥ pātu viśvataḥ ।। hiraṇyavarṇā jagatī jagamyāt । juṣatām iha pracetāḥ ।। vayāṣṭhaś ca sayujā yāv iha staḥ ।
svān mṛgān punar apy etu kṛṣṇaḥ ।। mṛgān kṛṣṇaḥ sacatāṃ vājo aśvam । saha yajñena payasā sacātai ।। namaḥ kṛṣṇāyota yo vājo asya ।
ayaṃ no vājī pra tirāty āyuḥ ।। ati yanty ahāny ati rātrīr aty uṣasaḥ । āpo antardhāvarīs tābhir antar dadhe tvā ।। bahvīḥ śuṣyanty oṣadhīḥ ।
yac ca paśyāmi yac ca na ।। hiraṇyavantam aṅkinam । ā lumpāmi mamed asan ।। anuvāka ।।
devā jīvā jīvyāsam aham । sarvam āyur jīvyāsam ।। tantyāṃ baddho divi śritaḥ । āhā tvā nirṛtaye ।।
rantir asi ramatir asi । mā śrutena vi rādhiṣi ।। viśvataḥ saṃdṛṣṭaḥ । somo asi rudro asi ।।
taṃ tvā yam ādityā aṃśum āpyāyanti । sa naḥ somaḥ pra tirad dīrgham āyuḥ ।। māsmākaṃ prāṇena । tasya prāṇenā pyāyasva ।।
cid asi samudrayoniḥ śyena ṛtāvān । rāyaspoṣeṇa prajayā dhanena ।। svarava stha namo vo mahatām ūrjāyai । parṇāṃ māva gām ।।
apaścāddaghvānnasya bhūyāsam । annādāyānnapataye rudrāya namo agnaye ।। yā te vaso vāta iṣuḥ sā ta eṣā । tayā no mṛḍa ।।
varuṇo grāvā marutaḥ pūtadakṣāḥ । takmanaḥ śocām apa nir nudantu ।। śayānam akovidam । -ānuṣṭhātā śivo bhava ।।
devayātur asi mṛḍo asi । yo asmān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ ।। brahmayātur asi mṛḍo asi । yo asmān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ ।।
annayātur asi mṛḍo asi । yo asmān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ ।। manuṣyayātur asi mṛḍo asi । yo asmān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ ।।
avabharaṇo nāmāsi devatrā ṇo akṣamāpaḥ । taṃ ta āsann api daghmaḥ ।। yad adosnātā āsuro dīkṣito acarat । -arasaṃ vṛścika te viṣam ।।
ketuluṅgā nāma te mātā karkaṭaḥ pitā । tat satyam arasam abhaga te viṣam ।। dve viṣasya dhāre striyā anyā puṃso anyā । te ubhe arase ।।
viśvavit taṃ naṣṭam anu paśyasi । ado me naṣṭaṃ tan me punar dehi ।। viśvakarman tat tvam upa gacchasi । ado me naṣṭaṃ tan me punar dehi ।।
viśvavyacas tat tvayy adhy āhitam । ado me naṣṭaṃ tan me punar dehi ।। dhastaṃ dadhātu dakṣiṇam । jīvena bhunajāmahai ।।
tat tvā goṣṭha ādadhāt । tad u rogam anīnaśat ।। viṣṇor manasā pūte sthaḥ । devo vāṃ savitot punātu ।।
devas tvā savitot punātu । sahasradhāreṇa supvā ।। viśvāni devo vayunāni vidvān । tebhyo juhomi sa juṣasva havyam ।।
agnāv agnir ity ekā ।। krimir vṛhati mūrdhataḥ । vīrut khanati bheṣajī ।। bhūrir nāmāsi rayir nāma ।
sa mā bhaga pra viśa । mṛje bhaga tvayi ।। ā mā gacchantu brahmacāriṇaḥ svāhā ।। carāṇi svāhā ।।
vi rājāni svāhā ।। asāni bhadrebhyaḥ śreyān svāhā ।। yaśasvī janutām anu carāṇi svāhā ।। paśūnāṃ brahmacāriṇām ।।
priyaṃ prajāpateḥ kṛṇu svāhā ।। hā amba panecari ।। tam u me agadaṃ kṛdhi ।। ubhayor akṣitasya ca ।।
udelaḍi ।। asur asi svāhā ।। kratur asi svāhā ।। puruṣo asi svāhā ।।
vijātir asi svāhā ।। prajātir asi svāhā ।। svajātir asi svāhā ।। svajātir nāmāsi svāhā ।।
tasya te yaśo bhakṣīya ।। tasya te madhu bhakṣīya ।। ihāsyāḥ śvaśuroyam asyāḥ śvaśuraḥ । adharā padyate nīcī padyate ।।
adhas padyatām adharā padyatāṃ nīcī padyatām । parājitāṃ praṇuttaitu paramāṃ parāvatam ।। praṇuttāṃ yatīm anvākśītām । parājita etv asāv āmuṣyāyaṇo amuṣyāḥ putraḥ ।।
asnā vyakta etu । aghaṃ hi raṇyetv asāv āmuṣyāyaṇo amuṣyāḥ putraḥ ।। aghapratīko aghenainaṃ vidhyāmaḥ । mṛtyor vyātta āsann api dadhāmi ।।
saṃrarāṇāḥ payasā saṃ babhūvuḥ । apāṃ prati prati gṛhṇātv enāḥ ।। svena mahasā yava । mā tvā divyāśanir vadhīt ।।
yatra tvācchāvadāmasi । samudra ivaidhy akṣitaḥ ।। akṣitāḥ santu rāśayaḥ । attāraḥ santv akṣitāḥ ।।
sakṛd bhūmir ajāyata । mā tvānu jani kaś cana ।। maṇiṃ kṛṇve sumaṅgalam । divānaktaṃ ca jīvase ।।
jambhayāmasi tvā vayam । yuvantaṃ kṣipantaṃ jahi ।। saṃkṣutaṃ duḥkṣutaṃ tubhyam astu । indra iva vṛtraṃ vajreṇa hantu ।।
parivādaṃ parikṣavam । parā tāṃ savitaḥ suva ।। puṇyaṃ bhakṣīmahi kṣavam । parṇakaś cābhi mehatām ।।
hastenādhāṃ sahīyasā । na vibhavāva kadā cana ।। asyasya svaṃkaram । yam ahaṃ kāmaye priyam ।।
cyavanaś cakra āsuraḥ । saṃ priyau bhavataṃ yuvam ।। saṃpriyau carato mṛgau । saṃpriyau bhavataṃ yuvam ।।
ā gṛhebhyaḥ svastaye । śatapatrābhi no vada ।। bhadram uttarato vada । bhadraṃ paścāt kapiñjala ।।
śunam uttarato vada । śunaṃ paścāt kapiñjala ।। jigyuṣām iva dundubhiḥ । śatapatrābhi no vada ।।
anuvāka ।। ud rathaṃ rathavāhanam । mayi gāvaś ca gopatau ।। un mitrāvaruṇāv aśvinobhā ।
viśāṃ patir upasattaidhy atra ।। tvaṃ deveṣūta mānuṣeṣu । asmākam astu pitṛṣu svadhāvat ।। asmabhyaṃ mṛgayadbhyaḥ ।
vāto hi raśanākṛtaḥ ।। sthāma gacchatu te punaḥ । tat prastambham ājatu । jaghanastambhinaṃ karaḥ ।।
hṛdayaṃ jihvayā saha । hikkām arasāṃ kṛdhi ।। anusṛptām ity ekā ।। pra patāta iti dve ।।
aśvāyeva tiṣṭhate ghāsam agne । agne mā te prativeśā riṣāma ।। aśvāyeva tiṣṭhate ghāsam asmai । mā te agne prativeśā riṣāma ।।
suvorjam iṣaṃ ca naḥ । āre bādhasva ducchunām ।। tisro vyuṣṭīr uṣasas te agne । tābhir naḥ pāhi sadam apramādam ।।
pāhi na uta dvitīyayā । pāhi catasṛbhir vaso ।। āyuṣmatyā ṛco mā chitsi । vasuvidaṃ lokam anu carāṇi ।।
ya ṛte cid ity ekā ।। mado nāmāsi mayi mādayāmum । agner adhi jāto asi brahmaṇā tejasā ca ।। sahānayā praviśehāntarā mām ।
-opa tvā hvaya upa mā hvayasva । nariṣṭā nāma vā asi ।। yathā māsā aharjaram । dhātar ā yantu sarvadā ।।
prastotāro māpa sthāta sumanyavaḥ । dṛḍhāso amariṣṇavo māvapiṣyavaḥ ।। savitā hastam agrahīt । -agnir ācāryas tava ।।
mama brahmacāry asi । svasti caratād ihāsau ।। sarvam asi sarvapate । svasti caratān mayi ।।
viśveṣāṃ kāmaś caratām ihāstu । -ā yantv anuvratā savitur daivyasya ।। punar aitu tanvā saṃvidānaḥ । mitro asmān varuṇa ubhayatas pātu ।।
idaṃ kṛṇmasi te haviḥ । athaitasya haviṣo vīhi svāhā ।। atho yad āñjana tvayi । ahaṃ bhūyāsam āñjana ।।
yadi vā svapnayānuśliṣṭam । asy abhidṛṣṭavīryam ।। ava varṣaṃ girer iva । hṛdi śliṣṭaṃ chinadmi te ।।
yac ca śliṣṭaṃ purītati । tat pārṣṇyāva chinadmi te ।। yac ca śiśne sanābhyām । pārṣṇir āśliṣṭāvacchedanī ।।
pārṣṇir āśliṣṭāvacchedanī । idam aham amuṣyāmuṣyāyaṇasyāmuṣyāḥ putrasyāśliṣṭāṃ pra cchinadmi ।। tad viṣṇuḥ punar ābharat । pumāṃsam asyai putraṃ dhehi svāhā ।।
yarjjarahastā cittyā । abhibhūr ṇo vipaścitā ।। pumān ayaṃ janiṣyate । sa pumān eva jāyatām ।।
bhadrāyākṣi vi vepatām । yad bhadraṃ tan na ā suva ।। ārtiṃ puruṣareṣiṇīm । apriye prati muñcatam ।।
aṅgādaṅgād avavepate । tasmān naḥ pātam aṃhasaḥ ।। ripram upeyima । mā no nv āgād aghaṃ yataḥ ।।
ariprā āpo apa ripram asmat । tasmin duṣvapnyam ā sṛjāmi ।। payo me vīrudho dadhan । payo me dadhat ।।
yasmin vratāny ādadhuḥ । somaṃ gacchantu no giraḥ ।। devām̐ acchā na majmanā । tasthau nākasya sānavi ।।
carkṛtyāni kṛṇvataḥ । -āgniṃ dhībhir duvasyata ।। viśvataḥ soma vṛṣṇyam । bhavā vājasya saṃgathe ।।
soma viśvebhir aṃśubhiḥ । bhavā naḥ sumnayuḥ sakhā vṛdhe ।। saṃ vṛṣṇyāny abhimātiṣāhaḥ । divi śravāṃsy uttamāni dhiṣva ।।
rājānaṃ ye tvā na viduḥ । prāṇena prajayā paśubhir gṛhair dhanenā pyāyasva । tayā tvam ā pyāyasva ।। cakṣuṣā śrotreṇa prāṇena prajayā paśubhir gṛhair dhanena ।।
veda devo bṛhaspatiḥ । tat satyaṃ cittamohanam ।। bhavena marutāṃ pitrā । vācaṃ vadiṣyato hatāḥ ।।
yad anyatra vivīṣatha । tad vaś cittam anīnaśam ।। nadīnāṃ ca niraṅkaśam । tena vaś cittam anīnaśam ।।
aṣṭau yāni manāṃsi ca । tad vaś cittam anīnaśam ।। -āgninā jātavedasā । tena vaś cittam anīnaśam ।।
aśvam ivāśvābhidhānyā । pador upānahau yathā ।। devānāṃ yātur asi । tayā mā jinva ।।
kaṇvā vidan mā gamaya । anu mā budhyantām ।। priyamedhā ṛṣayo nādhamānāḥ । mumugdhy asmān nidhayeva baddhān ।।
apsu jātasya mahatas pary aśmanaḥ । adbhiḥ parvata nāśaya ।। durgayonir vyadvarām । marīcīr anu nāśaya ।।
parṇe te vasatiṣ kṛtā । jahi vāmūn pra bādhama ।। parṇe te sadanaṃ kṛtam । jahi vāmūn pra bādhama ।।
vidhūya vipalāyate । amuṣmād adhy āyataḥ ।। sanir asi sanitāsi saneyam ।। kṛtir asi kartāsi kriyāsam ।।
vittir asi vettāsi videyam ।। bhūtir asi bhūtāsi bhūyāsam ।। bhūr asi subhūr asi subhūr nāmāsi ।। prajāpater madhyamaḥ śreṣṭho raśmir asi ।।
bhūtaye tvā vittaye tvā paśūnāṃ tvā vittaya ā dadhāmi ।। agnir vahnir vahnir agniḥ ।। indra āroddhā prajāpatiḥ pradātā ।। adabdhena tvā cakṣuṣāvekṣe ।।
ayuto me prāṇo ayuto me apāno ayuto ahaṃ sarvaḥ ।। devasya tvā savituḥ prasave aśvinor bāhubhyāṃ pūṣṇo hastābhyāṃ prasūta ā rabhe ।। agneṣ ṭvāsyena prāśnāmi bṛhaspater mukhena ।। indrasya tvā jaṭhare sādayāmi varuṇasyodare ।।
yo agnir nṛmaṇā nāma brāhmaṇeṣu praviṣṭaḥ ।। tan mā mā hiṃsīḥ parame vyoman ।। anuvāka ।। viśvaso nāma vā asi ।
śimidā nāma te svasā ।। giriṃ gaccheti sāptamikī ।। samudrād adhi māyayā । tad u rogam anīnaśat ।।
atho āsrāvabheṣajam । -āpi nahyāmi tā aham ।। dīkṣayā tapasā saha । punar indraḥ punar bhagaḥ ।
brahma jīvitavā adāt ।। uttānapādam arbhakaḥ । apa dveṣaḥ parā vahat ।। parāpataty āśumat ।
parā patati ketumat ।। saṃbharanti madhāv adhi । deveṣu puruṣeṣu ca ।। mahyā ariṣṭatātaye ।
etat puliśabheṣajam ।। agnī rakṣāṃsīty ekā ।। paiśeyaḥ peśyā hataḥ । vṛścikasyārasaṃ viṣam ।।
nir ut pucchād u te viṣam । tasyai te nama it sṛja ।। kim abhūd upaveśanam । agade kṛṇutā hanū ।।
divi candramasi śritam । māhaṃ pautram aghaṃ ni gām ।। ado vai tat prajāpatau । ।।
pṛthivyām adhi niṣṭhitam । ।। vidyut tat tvā tathā veda । māhaṃ pautram aghaṃ ni gām ।।
indrāgnī śarma yacchatam । prajānām adhipā vaśī ।। -ātmanaḥ parinirmitām । tām̐ agne jarase naya ।।
agnir iva jyotiṣā bṛhan । samudra iva duṣṭaraḥ ।। havir ojo yajur balam । vedaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ śacīpate ।।
ud bhare dyāvāpṛthivī sahauṣadhībhiḥ । gṛhṇāmi prajāṃ nir apaḥ sṛjāmi ।। mā brahma pra mathiṣṭana । upahūto ahaṃ sumedhā varcasvī ।।
mā no hiṃsiṣṭa yat tapaḥ । āpo bhavantu mātaraḥ ।। asmin goṣṭhe viśvabhṛto janitrīḥ । jānantu naḥ payasā ghṛtena ।।
mayi śrita stha mayi śrayadhvam । veda vo vittam ā mā viśata ।। vīra karmaṇikarmaṇi । yenedaṃ vivadāmahe ।।
takmānam uta rājayakṣmam । oṣadhyāṃ badhnāmi ।। pathe aham akaraṃ namaḥ ।। indrāya tviṣīmate pathe aham akaraṃ namaḥ ।।
pathe aham akaraṃ namaḥ ।। svasti punar ā naya । jīvā jyotir aśīmahi ।। satyaprāśaṃ purohitam ।
yo amum āmanasaṃ karat ।। -āroruvatka devaka । yam ahaṃ kāmaye priyam ।। ayaṃ no vasuvittamaḥ ।
-āyaṃ rakṣatu naḥ prajām ।। -aidhamānāḥ sve gṛhe । āyuṣmantaḥ suvarcasaḥ ।। kabrūr balāsabheṣajī ।
devī dadātu bheṣajam ।। tṛtīyasyām ito divi । śigruḥ kṣiptabheṣajaḥ ।। na śarva iṣum asyati ।
parvateṣu virohasi ।। girer anyo adhi pakṣasi । ā gantāṃ śigrutumburū ।। yāvanto adhyṛkṣarāḥ ।
tad u te viṣadūṣaṇam ।। jalāṇiti ।। asthād idam urv antarikṣam । hṛdayaṃ śamayāmi te ।।
saṃ māsau rohiṇī divaḥ । dīrgham āyuṣ kṛṇotu me ।। divā suparṇarohitau । -obhābhyām akaraṃ namaḥ ।।
namaḥ kumāraśatrave । namaḥ sabhāprapādine ।। gardabhāv abhitaḥsarau । namaḥ sabhāprapādine ।।
asāv eti pulīkayā । -odakaṃ parivācanam ।। parjanyād apa śīyate । abhīly apa śīyatām ।।
tvacaṃ me mābhi mimlapaḥ । -ābhīlīṃ nāśayāmasi ।। -ā pururūpād abhīlyaṃ mukhāt ।। āruroha malaṃ mukham ।
sūryas tad apa lumpatu ।। abhraṃ vātahṛtaṃ yathā । subhāgam astu me mukham ।। hiraṇyaṃ pratirocate ।
suvarṇaṃ prati rocatām ।। tveṣā vayāṃsy akraman । subhāgam astu me mukham ।। ulūkā saṃ pacāmi te ।।
ulūkā saṃ pacāmi te ।। ulūkā saṃ pacāmi te ।। ulūkāsaṃ pacāmi te ।। ulūkāsaṃ pacāmi te ।।
ulūkā saṃ pacāmi te ।। ulūkā saṃ pacāmi te ।। ulūkā saṃ pacāmi te ।। ulūkā saṃ pacāmi te ।।
ulūkā saṃ pacāmi te ।। dattāṃ somena babhruṇā । prāmuṣya hṛdayaṃ tapa ।। sam enaṃ takmanā sṛja ।
-āgniḥ parvāṇy anv ayad । muhūrtaṃ mām apaśyataḥ ।। vātas tvāta ud yamāt । -āsau hā iha te manaḥ ।।
vātas tvā yuṅktāṃ marutaś ca yuñjatām । arvāṅ ehi samaṭamāno marīcibhiḥ ।। pacāmi māṃsaṃ jvalayāmy asthi । mayi te ramatāṃ manaḥ ।।
smaraḥ pāñcalaḥ saṃtapanaḥ karaṃkaraḥ । yam ahaṃ kāmaye priyam ।। yathā tapati sūryaḥ । māṃ kāmena na ramāsā atra ।।
yathā vāsinakhādanam । yathā sūrya udyan sarvaṃ saṃtapati । māṃ kāmena na ramāsā atra ।। māṃ kāmena na ramāsā atra ।।
aṅgajvareṇocchocanīnām । viśvaśāradena mama kāmena ।। aty avādīd vaco mama । atrāre prāyasy astam ।।
cakre avāsā smaram । na suṣvāpa kadā cana । māva svāpsīt kadā cana ।। pari dyām eti sūryaḥ ।
mahyaṃ tapatu sarvataḥ ।। yathā tapati sūryaḥ । amuṃ mahyam ihā naya ।। vanād vananam ābhṛtam ।
apsarasāṃ samavānayat । ā mṛtyor ā parāvataḥ ।। anuvāka ।।
